beincrypto_1770733800000_1828253|1770733800000|2026|2|7|2026-02-10|beincrypto|Monero’s 65% Price Crash Didn’t Form a Bottom? Why $150 Is Now the Real Risk|<p><strong>The Monero price is down about 2% over the past 24 hours and nearly 31% over the past month. Since peaking near $799 in mid-January, XMR has already fallen more than 65%. A rebound followed the drop to $276, pushing the price back toward the $330 area. At first glance, this looked like stabilization after heavy selling.</strong></p>



<p>But a closer look tells a different story. </p>



<hr class="wp-block-separator has-alpha-channel-opacity" />



<h2 class="bic-gutenberg-heading wp-heading wp-block-heading" id="h-bear-flag-and-moving-averages-show-the-downtrend-is-still-intact">Bear Flag and Moving Averages Show the Downtrend Is Still Intact</h2>



<p>On the daily chart, <a href="https://beincrypto.com/monero-xmr-price-attempts-first-recovery/" rel="noreferrer noopener" target="_blank">Monero is trading </a>inside a bear flag structure.</p>



<p>A bear flag forms when the price drops sharply and then moves sideways or slightly higher in a narrow range. This pattern usually represents a pause before another decline, not a trend reversal. In XMR&rsquo;s case, the fall from $799 to $276 created the flagpole. The recent XMR price consolidation is forming a flag.</p>



<p>As long as the price remains inside this range, the dominant trend stays bearish. A breakdown below the lower boundary would likely trigger another major leg lower.</p>



<p>Trend indicators are reinforcing this view.</p>



<p>Exponential moving averages, or EMAs, are weighted price averages that give more importance to recent data. They help identify whether momentum is strengthening or weakening. When shorter-term EMAs fall below longer-term EMAs, it signals deteriorating trend strength.</p>



<p>Right now, Monero&rsquo;s 50-day EMA is moving toward the 100-day EMA. At the same time, the 20-day EMA is drifting toward the 200-day EMA.</p>



<figure class="wp-block-image size-full"><img alt="Bearish XMR Price Structure" class="wp-image-800716" src="https://assets.beincrypto.com/img/TGIBg61RMJZD1C_IMyAAyTg-WBY=/smart/68759f57d2954c059d57468133b2f5ae" /><figcaption class="wp-element-caption">Bearish XMR Price Structure<a href="https://www.tradingview.com/chart/HEOJm180/?symbol=KRAKEN%3AXMRUSD" rel="noreferrer noopener nofollow" target="_blank">: TradingView</a></figcaption></figure>



<p><em><strong>Want more token insights like this?&nbsp;Sign up for Editor Harsh Notariya&rsquo;s Daily Crypto Newsletter&nbsp;<a href="https://go.beincrypto.com/4lUzHZj" rel="noreferrer noopener" target="_blank">here</a>.</strong></em></p>



<p>These developing bearish crossovers suggest that short-term momentum continues to weaken relative to the broader trend. If these looming crossovers confirm while the XMR price flirts with the lower trendline of the flag, the breakdown theory would likely get validated.</p>



<hr class="wp-block-separator has-alpha-channel-opacity" />



<h2 class="bic-gutenberg-heading wp-heading wp-block-heading" id="h-spot-flows-show-rebounds-are-being-used-to-exit-not-accumulate">Spot Flows Show Rebounds Are Being Used to Exit, Not Accumulate?</h2>



<p>Exchange flow data reveals how investors are behaving during this consolidation.</p>



<p><a href="https://beincrypto.com/monero-price-44-percent-breakdown-risk/" rel="noreferrer noopener" target="_blank">In early February, Monero briefly showed</a> strong outflows (buying pressure). During the week ending February 2, net outflows reached about $7.1 million. This suggested that some buyers were stepping in after the crash.</p>



<p>But this support faded quickly.</p>



<p>By the week ending February 9, flows flipped to net inflows of around $768,000. More XMR was moving back onto exchanges than leaving them. This shift happened while the price dipped to $276 and then rebounded to the $327 zone.</p>



<figure class="wp-block-image size-full"><img alt="Positive Flows" class="wp-image-800719" src="https://assets.beincrypto.com/img/ZSGmK2wS2apNDyOus6jBHmFnRvs=/smart/726812f4b7d348589d8dbdaacacfd148" /><figcaption class="wp-element-caption">Positive Flows: <a href="https://www.coinglass.com/currencies/XMR/futures" rel="noreferrer noopener nofollow" target="_blank">Coinglass</a></figcaption></figure>



<p>This tells an important story. As soon as the price bounced, selling possibly resumed. Instead of holding for a recovery, many investors possibly used the rebound to reduce exposure. Loss exits replaced by accumulation.</p>



<p>When outflows turn into inflows during consolidation, it usually signals distribution. Supply is returning to the market. Without steady spot demand, rallies struggle to survive. This also explains why recent recoveries have been shallow. Buyers are not strong enough to absorb the returning supply.</p>



<p>With spot demand fading, the burden shifts to derivatives traders. But derivatives data show growing caution.</p>



<hr class="wp-block-separator has-alpha-channel-opacity" />



<h2 class="bic-gutenberg-heading wp-heading wp-block-heading" id="h-falling-open-interest-and-weak-funding-limit-the-xmr-recovery-potential">Falling Open Interest and Weak Funding Limit the XMR Recovery Potential</h2>



<p>Derivatives markets provide insight into trader confidence and leverage. Open interest measures the total value of active futures contracts. Rising open interest shows that traders are building positions. Falling open interest shows that traders are closing positions and stepping away.</p>



<p>In mid-January, Monero&rsquo;s open interest stood near $279 million. By February 10, it had dropped to around $110 million. This represents a decline of more than 60%.</p>



<figure class="wp-block-image size-full"><img alt="Open Interest Resets" class="wp-image-800718" src="https://assets.beincrypto.com/img/-GufY9BHI6_fRCa797vVRjrpqFY=/smart/bf227ad61c8944a8bade7b2daf7fa426" /><figcaption class="wp-element-caption">Open Interest Resets:<a href="https://www.coinglass.com/currencies/XMR/futures" rel="noreferrer noopener nofollow" target="_blank"> Coinglass</a></figcaption></figure>



<p>Such a sharp drop indicates that leverage is leaving the market. Traders are reducing risk rather than preparing for a major rebound.</p>



<p>At the same time, funding rates remain mildly positive. Funding rates reflect the cost traders pay to hold futures positions. When funding is positive, long traders are dominant. When it is negative, short traders dominate.</p>



<p>XMR&rsquo;s funding remains slightly positive, meaning most remaining traders still lean bullish. But without rising open interest, this bias lacks conviction.</p>



<figure class="wp-block-image size-full"><img alt="Weighted Funding Rate For XMR" class="wp-image-800722" src="https://assets.beincrypto.com/img/lWuY90Ihl0cfGlLWmsEaYyoO1yk=/smart/69cd96ee0d4d473cbc2cedb8e2ec9c4f" /><figcaption class="wp-element-caption">Weighted Funding Rate For XMR: <a href="https://www.coinglass.com/currencies/XMR/futures" rel="noreferrer noopener nofollow" target="_blank">Coinglass</a></figcaption></figure>



<p>This combination is weak. Fewer traders are participating, yet optimism has not fully reset.  It also limits the chance of a short squeeze. A short squeeze requires heavy bearish positioning. Without that pressure, upside accelerations are unlikely.</p>



<p>With leverage shrinking and spot buyers hesitant, the price lacks fuel for sustained recovery.</p>



<hr class="wp-block-separator has-alpha-channel-opacity" />



<h2 class="bic-gutenberg-heading wp-heading wp-block-heading" id="h-why-150-is-becoming-key-target-for-the-monero-price">Why $150 Is Becoming Key Target for the Monero Price</h2>



<p>With technical, spot, and derivatives signals aligned, downside levels become increasingly important.</p>



<p>The first major support sits near $314. This area aligns with recent lows and the lower boundary of the bear flag. A decisive break below it would likely confirm continuation lower.</p>



<p>If $314 fails, downside opens quickly.</|https://beincrypto.com/monero-price-crash-prediction-150-target/|layer2,whale,selloff|ETH,SOL,NEAR,OP,TRX|negative|0.6|1770720436053

<p>The debate carries significant implications for traders and investors navigating Bitcoin&rsquo;s volatility in early 2026.</p>



<h2 class="bic-gutenberg-heading wp-heading wp-block-heading" id="h-bitcoin-is-following-its-4-year-cycle-amid-sharp-correction">Bitcoin Is Following Its 4-Year Cycle Amid Sharp Correction</h2>



<p>Bitcoin fell from its cycle <a href="https://beincrypto.com/bitcoin-all-time-high-126k-retail-price-cycle-questions/" rel="noreferrer noopener" target="_blank">peak near $126,000</a> to the $60,000&ndash;<a href="https://beincrypto.com/bitcoin-70k-pump-or-crash-analysis/" rel="noreferrer noopener" target="_blank">$70,000 range in early </a>February. This marked a drawdown of roughly 52%. </p>



<p>While the move rattled market sentiment, Kaiko argues the decline is fully consistent with previous post-halving bear markets and does not signal a structural break from historical patterns.</p>



<blockquote class="max-w-xl text-4.5 border-l-2 border-blue-600 pl-11 mb-9 select-all [&amp;_p]:!mb-0 wp-block-quote is-layout-flow wp-block-quote-is-layout-flow">
<p>&ldquo;Bitcoin&rsquo;s decline from $126,000 to $60,000 confirms rather than contradicts the four-year halving cycle, which has consistently delivered 50-80% drawdowns following cycle peaks,&rdquo; Kaiko&rsquo;s data debrief read.</p>
</blockquote>



<p>The report notes that the 2024 halving took place in April. Bitcoin topped out roughly 12&ndash;18 months later, aligning closely with prior cycles. In past instances, such peaks have typically been followed by extended bear markets lasting around a year before the next accumulation phase begins.&nbsp;</p>



<figure class="wp-block-image size-full"><img alt="Bitcoin's 4-Year Halving Cycle." class="wp-image-800695" src="https://assets.beincrypto.com/img/H6YfOutEBCCSHTvwH5JleSGpa_4=/smart/a54f22abbc8242768bd8dbf7d038cdda" /><figcaption class="wp-element-caption">Bitcoin&rsquo;s 4-Year Halving Cycle. Source: <a href="https://research.kaiko.com/insights" rel="noreferrer noopener nofollow" target="_blank">Kaiko</a></figcaption></figure>



<p>Kaiko says the current price action suggests Bitcoin has transitioned out of the euphoric post-halving phase and into that expected corrective period.</p>



<p>It is worth noting that many experts have <a href="https://beincrypto.com/bitcoin-four-year-cycle-analysis/" rel="noreferrer noopener" target="_blank">previously challenged</a> Bitcoin&rsquo;s 4-year cycle. They argue that it no longer holds in today&rsquo;s market. In October, <a href="https://beincrypto.com/arthur-hayes-bitcoins-4-year-cycle-is-dead-long-live-liquidity/" rel="noreferrer noopener" target="_blank">Arthur Hayes said the 4-year</a> Bitcoin cycle was over. He pointed instead to global liquidity as the dominant driver of price movements.</p>



<p>Others have argued that Bitcoin now follows a<a href="https://beincrypto.com/bitcoin-market-cycle-institutional-liquidity-outlook-2026/" rel="noreferrer noopener" target="_blank"> </a>5<a href="https://beincrypto.com/bitcoin-market-cycle-institutional-liquidity-outlook-2026/" rel="noreferrer noopener" target="_blank">-year cycle rather</a> than a 4-year one. They cite the growing influence of global liquidity conditions, institutional participation, and broader macroeconomic policy shifts.</p>



<p>Kaiko acknowledged that structural changes, including spot Bitcoin <a href="https://beincrypto.com/learn/what-is-bitcoin-etf/" rel="noreferrer noopener" target="_blank">exchange-traded fund (ETF)</a> adoption, greater regulatory clarity, and a more mature DeFi ecosystem, have distinguished 2024-2025 from previous cycles.&nbsp;Nonetheless, it said these developments have not prevented the expected post-peak retracement.</p>



<p>Instead, they have changed how volatility manifests. Spot Bitcoin ETFs recorded more than $2.1 billion in outflows during the recent sell-off. </p>



<p>This amplified downside pressure and demonstrated that institutional access increases liquidity in both directions, not just on the way up. According to Kaiko,</p>



<blockquote class="max-w-xl text-4.5 border-l-2 border-blue-600 pl-11 mb-9 select-all [&amp;_p]:!mb-0 wp-block-quote is-layout-flow wp-block-quote-is-layout-flow">
<p>&ldquo;While DeFi infrastructure has shown relative resilience compared to 2022, TVL declines and slowing staking flows indicate no sector is immune to bear market dynamics. Regulatory clarity&nbsp;has proven insufficient to decouple crypto from broader macro risk factors, with Fed uncertainty and risk-asset weakness dominating market direction.&rdquo;&nbsp;</p>
</blockquote>



<p>Kaiko also raised the key question now <a href="https://beincrypto.com/bitcoin-bottom-prediction-analysts-key-levels/" rel="noreferrer noopener" target="_blank">dominating market discussions:</a> where is the bottom? The report explained that Bitcoin&rsquo;s intraday rebound from $60,000 to $70,000 suggests initial support may be forming.&nbsp;</p>



<p>However, historical precedent shows that <a href="https://beincrypto.com/learn/bear-market-signs/" rel="noreferrer noopener" target="_blank">bear markets typically </a>take six to 12 months and involve multiple failed rallies before a sustainable bottom is established.</p>



<p>Kaiko noted that stablecoin dominance stands at 10.3%, while funding rates have fallen close to zero and futures open interest has dropped by about 55%, signaling significant deleveraging across the market. Still, the firm cautioned that it remains unclear whether current conditions represent early, mid, or late-stage capitulation.</p>



<blockquote class="max-w-xl text-4.5 border-l-2 border-blue-600 pl-11 mb-9 select-all [&amp;_p]:!mb-0 wp-block-quote is-layout-flow wp-block-quote-is-layout-flow">
<p>&ldquo;The four-year cycle framework predicts we should be at the 30% mark. Bitcoin is doing exactly what it has done in every previous cycle, but it seems many market participants&nbsp;convinced themselves this time would be different,&rdquo; Kaiko wrote.</p>
</blockquote>



<p>As February 2026 progresses, market participants must weigh both sides of this argument. Bitcoin&rsquo;s next moves will reveal whether history continues to repeat or a new market regime is taking shape.</p>

Traders started discussing a possible trend reversal.</strong></p>



<p>But blockchain data tells a different story. Instead of showing strong accumulation, on-chain metrics suggest that many holders used the rebound to exit losing positions. Selling at a loss remains dominant. Several groups are still reducing exposure. This raises a key question: was the bounce genuine demand, or simply exit liquidity for trapped sellers?</p>



<hr class="wp-block-separator has-alpha-channel-opacity" />



<h2 class="bic-gutenberg-heading wp-heading wp-block-heading" id="h-technical-setup-shows-bounce-potential-but-it-needs-confirmation">Technical Setup Shows Bounce Potential, But It Needs Confirmation</h2>



<p>On the 12-hour chart, XRP is trading inside a falling wedge pattern, with a 56% breakout potential above the upper trendline.</p>



<p>For this pattern to activate, <a href="https://beincrypto.com/ripple-expands-custody-partnerships-xrp-price-struggles/" rel="noreferrer noopener" target="_blank">XRP needs</a> to first reclaim its short-term moving average, the 20-period exponential moving average (EMA), which gives more weight to recent prices. This level acts as dynamic resistance in downtrends. In early January, a clean break above this EMA triggered a rally of nearly 30%.</p>



<p>Momentum is also showing early improvement.</p>



<p>Between January 31 and February 9, XRP printed a lower low in price. At the same time, the Relative Strength Index (RSI), a momentum indicator that measures buying and selling pressure, formed a higher low. This bullish divergence suggests that sellers are losing strength.</p>



<figure class="wp-block-image size-full"><img alt="XRP Price Structure" class="wp-image-800648" src="https://assets.beincrypto.com/img/059-ipYmZgAx254v_FNVUEWwbRI=/smart/26ff370b28364303afe4344ca012211c" /><figcaption class="wp-element-caption">XRP Price Structure: <a href="https://www.tradingview.com/chart/HEOJm180/?symbol=COINBASE%3AXRPUSD" rel="noreferrer noopener nofollow" target="_blank">TradingView</a></figcaption></figure>



<p><em><strong>Want more token insights like this?&nbsp;Sign up for Editor Harsh Notariya&rsquo;s Daily Crypto Newsletter&nbsp;<a href="https://go.beincrypto.com/4lUzHZj" rel="noreferrer noopener" target="_blank">here</a>.</strong></em></p>



<p>On its own, this setup points to a possible bounce.</p>



<p>But technical patterns only work when holders are willing to stay invested. To understand whether this bounce has real support, we need to look at how investors are behaving on-chain.</p>



<hr class="wp-block-separator has-alpha-channel-opacity" />



<h2 class="bic-gutenberg-heading wp-heading wp-block-heading" id="h-sopr-shows-holders-are-still-selling-at-losses-despite-the-bounce">SOPR Shows Holders Are Still Selling at Losses Despite the Bounce</h2>



<p>One of the clearest warning signals comes from the Spent Output Profit Ratio, or SOPR. SOPR measures whether coins being moved on-chain are sold in profit or at a loss. When it stays above 1, it shows profit-taking. When it remains below 1, it shows loss-selling.</p>



<p>Since late January, XRP&rsquo;s SOPR has remained below 1 for more than ten consecutive days.</p>



<figure class="wp-block-image size-full"><img alt="SOPR Under 1" class="wp-image-800650" src="https://assets.beincrypto.com/img/NszXUyMcYq-24uCU3T4XjuJIwBE=/smart/61c57c8ee6924876a5771f7f6e250766" /><figcaption class="wp-element-caption">SOPR Under 1: <a href="https://studio.glassnode.com/dashboards/asset-overview?a=XRP&amp;referrer=home_assets_table" rel="noreferrer noopener nofollow" target="_blank">Glassnode</a></figcaption></figure>



<p>This is unusual. After a 30%+ rebound, short-term traders are normally sitting in profit. That usually pushes SOPR higher. But in XRP&rsquo;s case, profitability never returned. Loss selling continued even as the price recovered. This means many holders are still exiting underwater positions.</p>



<p>In simple terms, the market is not seeing confident profit-taking. It is seeing stress-driven exits. To understand who is responsible, we need to look at holder cohorts.</p>



<hr class="wp-block-separator has-alpha-channel-opacity" />



<h2 class="bic-gutenberg-heading wp-heading wp-block-heading" id="h-holder-data-confirms-the-xrp-bounce-is-being-used-to-exit-not-accumulate">Holder Data Confirms the XRP Bounce Is Being Used to Exit, Not Accumulate</h2>



<p>HODL Waves group XRP wallets based on how long they have held their coins. This helps identify which investor groups are buying or selling.</p>



<p>The most striking shift appeared in the 24-hour holder cohort.</p>



<p>On February 6, this group controlled about 1% of XRP&rsquo;s circulating supply. Within days, that share collapsed to roughly 0.09%. That represents a decline of more than 90%.</p>



<figure class="wp-block-image size-full"><img alt="Speculative Holders Bought The Top?" class="wp-image-800652" src="https://assets.beincrypto.com/img/4mdkLtvAn_37QK0Et0S5QDVzBXk=/smart/38475f540a354e539711ce5d245900b5" /><figcaption class="wp-element-caption">Speculative Holders Bought The Top?: <a href="https://studio.glassnode.com/dashboards/asset-overview?a=XRP&amp;referrer=home_assets_table" rel="noreferrer noopener nofollow" target="_blank">Glassnode</a></figcaption></figure>



<p>These were highly reactive traders who entered during volatility and rushed to exit during the rebound.</p>



<p>Selling was not limited to this group.</p>



<p>The 1-month to 3-month cohort, which accumulated heavily in January when <a href="https://beincrypto.com/xrp-price-bottom-signal-analysis/" rel="noreferrer noopener" target="_blank">XRP traded</a> near $2.07, has also been reducing exposure. Their share of supply fell from around 14.48% in mid-January to about 9.48% recently. That is a decline of roughly 35%.</p>



<figure class="wp-block-image size-full"><img alt="Mid-Term XRP Holders Selling" class="wp-image-800653" src="https://assets.beincrypto.com/img/J0DIvdaxKF5IY3KHvjAr4Wighcs=/smart/2aa3010c8b0f41c4b3fecc3165cca0b7" /><figcaption class="wp-element-caption">Mid-Term XRP Holders Selling:<a href="https://studio.glassnode.com/dashboards/asset-overview?a=XRP&amp;referrer=home_assets_table" rel="noreferrer noopener nofollow" target="_blank"> Glassnode</a></figcaption></figure>



<p>These holders remain underwater. Instead of waiting for a full recovery, they are using rallies to minimize losses. Together, these two cohorts explain why SOPR has remained depressed for a long time now.</p>



<p>Short-term traders are exiting failed trades. Medium-term holders are cutting losing positions.</p>



<p>This behavior is typical of distribution phases, not early bull markets. And it directly impacts price structure.</p>



<hr class="wp-block-separator has-alpha-channel-opacity" />



<h2 class="bic-gutenberg-heading wp-heading wp-block-heading" id="h-cost-basis-data-shows-why-1-44-1-54-is-a-wall-for-the-xrp-price">Cost Basis Data Shows Why $1.44&ndash;$1.54 Is a Wall for the XRP Price</h2>



<p>Cost basis heat maps show where large groups of investors bought their coins. These zones often become resistance when the price returns to them.</p>



<p>For XRP, the strongest near-term cluster sits between $1.42 and $1.44. More than 660 million XRP were accumulated in this range. This creates a powerful sell zone.</p>



<figure class="wp-block-image size-full"><img alt="Key Sell Wall" class="wp-image-800656" src="https://assets.beincrypto.com/img/EhzNwQezqFtAnSr5VRjXQDGSM9M=/smart/50f2864350ec46eca7699728dbee5916" /><figcaption class="wp-element-caption">Key Sell Wall: <a href="https://studio.glassnode.com/da|https://beincrypto.com/xrp-price-bounce-analysis-sellers-exit/|regulation,exchange,whale,selloff,pump|ETH,SOL,NEAR,XRP,TRX|neutral|0.8|1770720436056

Notably, Coinbase is revered as the largest US-based exchange by trading volume.</strong></p>



<p>Hyperliquid&rsquo;s ascent is forcing the crypto industry to reassess long-held assumptions about where serious trading activity takes place.</p>



<h2 class="bic-gutenberg-heading wp-heading wp-block-heading" id="h-hyperliquid-surpasses-coinbase-in-trading-volume">Hyperliquid Surpasses Coinbase in Trading Volume</h2>



<p>According to Artemis, Hyperliquid recorded roughly $2.6 trillion in <a href="https://beincrypto.com/bitcoin-ethereum-options-expiry-volatility-2026/" rel="noreferrer noopener" target="_blank">notional trading volume</a>, compared with $1.4 trillion for Coinbase, meaning nearly double the activity.</p>



<p>The figures mark one of the clearest signals yet that high-performance on-chain platforms are capturing a growing share of global derivatives flows.</p>



<figure class="wp-block-image size-full"><img alt="Coinbase versus Hyperliquid Trading Volume" class="wp-image-800649" src="https://assets.beincrypto.com/img/t0HjA-WFGuR_XaDgveKxcjECTgA=/smart/9b6ba7beb1d64392a3366159d46574fc" /><figcaption class="wp-element-caption">Coinbase versus Hyperliquid Trading Volume. <p>This milestone fuels debate over whether decentralized trading venues are beginning to rival centralized exchanges in scale and influence.</p>



<blockquote class="max-w-xl text-4.5 border-l-2 border-blue-600 pl-11 mb-9 select-all [&amp;_p]:!mb-0 wp-block-quote is-layout-flow wp-block-quote-is-layout-flow">

</blockquote>



<p>The gap is not limited to trading volumes. Year-to-date performance data shows a striking divergence between the two companies.</p>



<p>Hyperliquid is up 31.7%, while Coinbase is down 27.0%, creating a 58.7<strong>% </strong>performance gap in just a matter of weeks.</p>



<p>For analysts, this divergence reflects deeper structural shifts rather than short-term volatility. Anthony, a data analyst at Artemis, emphasized that underlying metrics are increasingly driving market sentiment.</p>

<p>The comment highlights a growing belief among market observers that liquidity, execution quality, and user activity are beginning to shape valuations and investor narratives. This is as opposed to brand recognition alone.</p>



<p>One question raised by the data is why Binance, the <a href="https://beincrypto.com/binance-safu-fund-btc-accumulation-market-signal/" rel="noreferrer noopener" target="_blank">world&rsquo;s largest crypto derivatives exchange</a>, was not included in the comparison.</p>



<p>The reason lies in what the figures are measuring and the narrative surrounding them. The Artemis analysis focused on Hyperliquid overtaking Coinbase, a major centralized exchange whose business is heavily weighted toward spot trading and regulated markets.</p>



<p>The milestone, therefore, highlights a shift in market structure rather than a direct challenge to the largest derivatives venue.</p>



<p>Binance remains the dominant player in perpetual futures trading by a wide margin. Coingecko data shows the exchange processing over $53 billion in daily derivatives volume. This exceeds Hyperliquid&rsquo;s $6.4 billion.</p>

<h2 class="bic-gutenberg-heading wp-heading wp-block-heading" id="h-hyperliquid-s-surge-sparks-a-new-fight-over-who-controls-crypto-trading">Hyperliquid&rsquo;s Surge Sparks a New Fight Over Who Controls Crypto Trading</h2>



<p>The data has sparked strong reactions across the crypto community, highlighting long-standing tensions between centralized and decentralized trading models.</p>



<p>To some, Hyperliquid&rsquo;s rise is a validation of on-chain markets, while others used the moment to criticize centralized exchanges.</p>



<figure class="wp-block-embed is-type-rich is-provider-twitter wp-block-embed-twitter"><div class="wp-block-embed__wrapper">

</div></figure>



<p>Such criticism reflects a broader sentiment among some traders who argue that transparent, on-chain systems reduce counterparty risk and improve market fairness.</p>



<p>However, defenders of centralized exchanges note that they still dominate in fiat on-ramps, regulatory integration, and retail accessibility.</p>



<p>Perhaps the most significant implication of Hyperliquid&rsquo;s growth is how it is changing the competitive sector. Rather than being compared primarily with other <a href="https://beincrypto.com/gate-launches-precious-metals-futures/" rel="noreferrer noopener" target="_blank">perpetual DEXs</a>, the platform is increasingly being measured against major centralized derivatives venues.</p>



<p>Hyperliquid Hub, a community account tracking the ecosystem, argued that the platform has already pulled ahead of most decentralized rivals.</p>

</blockquote>



<p>If this perception continues to gain traction, it could mark a turning point in how traders evaluate execution venues. It is less about whether they are centralized or decentralized and more about liquidity, speed, and reliability.</p>

<h2 class="bic-gutenberg-heading wp-heading wp-block-heading" id="h-ripple-expands-custody-offering-with-figment-and-securosys-partnerships-nbsp">Ripple Expands Custody Offering With Figment and Securosys Partnerships&nbsp;</h2>



<p>Ripple said <a href="https://beincrypto.com/ripple-dxc-digital-asset-banking-partnership/" rel="noreferrer noopener" target="_blank">the partnerships are designed </a>to simplify procurement and support faster deployment of custody services for regulated institutions. <p>As part of the partnership with Figment, Ripple will introduce staking functionality. This will allow institutional clients to offer staking services without operating their own validator infrastructure.&nbsp;</p>



<p>The integration is aimed at banks, custodians, and <a href="https://beincrypto.com/learn/ripple-vs-sec/" rel="noreferrer noopener" target="_blank">regulated entities seeking </a>exposure to Proof-of-Stake networks while maintaining institutional security and governance standards.</p>



<p>Through Figment&rsquo;s infrastructure, Ripple Custody clients will be able to support staking on major networks such as Ethereum (ETH) <a href="https://beincrypto.com/solana-price-prediction-unstaking-crash-risk/" rel="noreferrer noopener" target="_blank">and Solana (SOL).</a>&nbsp;</p>



<blockquote class="max-w-xl text-4.5 border-l-2 border-blue-600 pl-11 mb-9 select-all [&amp;_p]:!mb-0 wp-block-quote is-layout-flow wp-block-quote-is-layout-flow">

</blockquote>



<p>Separately, Ripple has partnered with Securosys to strengthen the security layer of Ripple Custody. The collaboration adds support for CyberVault HSM and CloudHSM. This gives institutions the option to deploy HSM-based custody either on premises or in the cloud.</p>



<p>According to Ripple, the Securosys integration is designed to address long-standing challenges around HSM adoption. This includes cost, complexity, and slow procurement processes.&nbsp;</p>



<p>Ripple also noted that the addition of Securosys expands the range of supported HSM providers on its custody platform. This provides greater flexibility for institutions operating across multiple regulatory environments.</p>



<blockquote class="max-w-xl text-4.5 border-l-2 border-blue-600 pl-11 mb-9 select-all [&amp;_p]:!mb-0 wp-block-quote is-layout-flow wp-block-quote-is-layout-flow">
<p>&ldquo;By integrating our CyberVault HSM with Ripple Custody, institutions gain an out-of-the-box, enterprise-grade solution that can be deployed quickly, without added complexity, while retaining full control over their cryptographic keys,&rdquo; Robert Rogenmoser, CEO of Securosys, remarked.</p>

newsbtc_1770739252000_9045604|1770739252000|2026|2|7|2026-02-10|newsbtc|Bitcoin Could See New Drop To $60,000 Despite Bounce – Here’s The Level To Defend|<p style="font-weight: 400;">As the crypto market recovers from last week’s correction, Bitcoin (BTC) is attempting to reclaim a crucial price zone. Despite the bounce, some analysts have warned that the bottom may not be in yet, suggesting the flagship crypto could soon retest its recent lows.</p>

<h2 style="font-weight: 400;">Bitcoin Bottom Below $60,000, Says Analyst</h2>
<p style="font-weight: 400;">On Monday, Bitcoin continued its sideways move, trying to turn a key area into support for the third consecutive day. After hitting a two-year low of $60,000 last week, the flagship crypto has bounced 17.5% to trade between $68,000 and $72,000 over the past few days.</p>
<p style="font-weight: 400;">Nonetheless, the cryptocurrency has failed to reclaim the upper zone of its short-term price range, raising questions about the <a href="https://www.newsbtc.com/analysis/btc/bitcoin-price-cools-above-70k/" rel="noopener " target="_blank">direction</a> of BTC’s next move.</p>
<p style="font-weight: 400;">As the price recovered, Crypto Bullet noted that the BTC printed a “strong weekly close” above the 200-week Exponential Moving Average (EMA), leaving Thursday’s correction as a long wick.</p>
<p style="font-weight: 400;">The analyst cautioned that these wicks have usually been filled the following week, pointing to the late February 2025 and early October 2025 corrections and the subsequent performance.</p>
<img alt="Bitcoin" class="size-large wp-image-880595" height="474" src="https://www.newsbtc.com/wp-content/uploads/2026/02/HAtFeOfb0AAPT0v.jpeg?w=860&#038;resize=860%2C474" width="860" />
<p style="font-weight: 400;">Based on this, he suggested that Bitcoin could retest the $60,000 area again, where the 200-week Moving Average (MA) is also located. Similarly, Ted Pillows <a href="https://x.com/TedPillows/status/2020793544689234109?s=20" rel="noopener nofollow" target="_blank">highlighted</a> BTC’s Monday bounce above $70,000, asserting that the key level to defend is the $68,000 support, where the EMA200 sits.</p>
<p style="font-weight: 400;"> If the price fails to hold this level, the market observer suggested a deeper correction could be expected, with Bitcoin risking a drop below the recent lows if that level also fails to hold.</p>
<p style="font-weight: 400;">Meanwhile, Ali Martinez <a href="https://x.com/alicharts/status/2020884393464869046?s=20" rel="noopener nofollow" target="_blank">hinted</a> that BTC’s bottom might not be in, as “Bitcoin has historically bottomed around the −1.0 MVRV Pricing Band.” According to the chart shared on X, that level currently sits at $52,040.</p>
<h2 style="font-weight: 400;">BTC To See Leeser Relief Rally?</h2>
<p style="font-weight: 400;">Another market watcher highlighted BTC’s macro descending triangle pattern, which it has been <a href="https://www.newsbtc.com/news/bitcoin-to-30000-analysts-warn-btc-crash-could-be-deeper-than-expected/" rel="noopener " target="_blank">forming</a> in the monthly timeframe since mid-2024, suggesting that its potential bounce could be a “lesser relief rally compared to the 2024-2025 advance to the upside.”</p>
<p style="font-weight: 400;">Rekt Capital <a href="https://newsletter.rektcapital.co/whats-next-for-bitcoin/" rel="noopener nofollow" target="_blank">noted</a> that upon breakdown from its macro triangles, Bitcoin tends to react from the 50-Month EMA. However, it has historically been followed by a downside deviation below this level.</p>
<p style="font-weight: 400;">“When viewed through the lens of the Macro Descending Triangle, history shows that Bitcoin has consistently failed to revisit the base of the Macro Triangle following breakdowns, which means BTC may fall short of $82.5k on any upcoming relief rally.”</p>
<p style="font-weight: 400;">To the analyst, if BTC can build <a href="https://www.newsbtc.com/bitcoin-news/major-problem-after-bitcoin-drop/" rel="noopener " target="_blank">support</a> above the $71,000 area, where the post-halving accumulation breakout occurred, the price could attempt a move into the mid-$70,000.</p>

<p style="font-weight: 400;">However, the flagship crypto “is still negotiating whether it will locate itself within the Post-Halving Range,” and has not decisively reclaimed the upper zone of its current range as support, “is instead showing early signs of flipping into resistance on the Weekly timeframe.”</p>
<p style="font-weight: 400;">As a result, Bitcoin could consolidate around its post-halving range again if the $70,000 mark confirms as resistance. “At roughly 30% of the way through this part of the market cycle, there remains ample time for further structural movement to unfold but history suggests whatever clustering develops will likely be distributive before continuing additional Bearish Acceleration,” Rekt Capital concluded.</p>
<img alt="bitcoin, btc, btcusdt" class="size-large wp-image-880594" height="613" src="https://www.newsbtc.com/wp-content/uploads/2026/02/BTCUSDT_2026-02-09_13-59-10.png?w=860&#038;resize=860%2C613" width="860" />|https://www.newsbtc.com/news/bitcoin/bitcoin-new-drop-60000-despite-bounce-level-defend/|regulation,whale,mining,selloff,pump|BTC,ETH,SOL,TRX|negative|1.0|1770720436337
newsbtc_1770738868000_9926148|1770738868000|2026|2|7|2026-02-10|newsbtc|Bitcoin ETFs Extend Inflow Streak as Institutional Capital Rotates Into $HYPER|<p><strong>What to Know:</strong></p>
<ul>
<li>Spot Bitcoin ETFs continue to see consistent net inflows, creating a supply shock that historically precedes capital rotation into infrastructure altcoins.</li>
<li>Bitcoin Hyper differentiates itself by integrating the Solana Virtual Machine (SVM) to bring high-speed, programmable smart contracts to the Bitcoin network.</li>
<li>The project solves Bitcoin’s core limitations of slow transactions and high fees while preserving the security guarantees of the Layer 1 blockchain.</li>
</ul>

<p>Institutional appetite for digital assets isn&#8217;t showing any signs of slowing down. Spot Bitcoin ETFs just logged <strong><a href="https://sosovalue.com/assets/etf/Total_Crypto_Spot_ETF_Fund_Flow?page=usBTC" rel="noopener nofollow" target="_blank">another week of consistent net inflows</a></strong>, signaling a distinct shift in market structure.</p>
<p><img alt="Sosovalue data showing consistent ETF inflows." class="aligncenter wp-image-880671" height="250" src="https://www.newsbtc.com/wp-content/uploads/2026/02/sosovalue0data-showing-consistent-etf-inflows.jpg?w=750&#038;resize=700%2C250" width="700" /></p>
<p>The data points to a supply shock dynamic where issuers like BlackRock and Fidelity are absorbing coins faster than miners can produce them, effectively creating a rising price floor for the premier asset.</p>
<p>That stability matters. Historically, when Bitcoin goes flat after a run, liquidity trickles down to high-beta infrastructure plays, specifically the ones solving Bitcoin’s scaling headaches. While Bitcoin remains the pristine collateral of the crypto economy, its network congestion and lack of programmability are still major barriers to mass adoption.</p>
<p>Investors are now looking past the store-of-value narrative toward the execution layer. The market is hunting for protocols that can unlock the nearly $2T of dormant capital on the Bitcoin network. Amidst this search for yield, <a href="https://newsbtc.care/box_7271b6427956901b28f9e1ee77c086e1" rel="noopener nofollow" target="_blank"><strong>Bitcoin Hyper ($HYPER)</strong></a> has emerged as a focal point for developers and smart money alike.</p>
<p>By integrating the speed of the Solana Virtual Machine (SVM) directly with Bitcoin’s security architecture, the project is positioning itself to capture the liquidity overflowing from the ETF-driven bull market.</p>
<h2>Solving The Execution Bottleneck: SVM Meets Bitcoin Security</h2>
<p>The current landscape of Bitcoin Layer 2s is a bit of a mess. Users are often forced to choose between speed and security. Bitcoin Hyper fixes this dichotomy with a modular architecture: it uses the Bitcoin L1 for final settlement while deploying a real-time SVM Layer 2 for execution.</p>
<p><img alt="Bitcoin Hyper L2 explained." class="aligncenter wp-image-878766" height="456" src="https://www.newsbtc.com/wp-content/uploads/2026/02/Screenshot-2026-02-02-10.54.58.png?w=750&#038;resize=700%2C456" width="700" /></p>
<p>That’s a massive technical differentiator. By using the Solana Virtual Machine, the network achieves low-latency processing and high throughput that native Bitcoin script simply can&#8217;t support.</p>
<p>For developers, this integration changes the calculus of building on Bitcoin. The protocol supports Rust-based smart contracts, allowing dApps to run with the performance users expect from modern DeFi, while anchoring their state to Bitcoin’s immutable ledger.</p>
<p>This &#8216;best of both worlds&#8217; approach, Solana’s speed plus Bitcoin’s trust, aims to solve the friction of high fees and slow block times that have historically plagued the ecosystem.</p>
<p>The utility here extends beyond simple transfers. The infrastructure supports a decentralized Canonical Bridge for seamless $BTC transfers and offers a robust environment for NFT platforms and gaming dApps. By enabling high-speed payments in wrapped BTC and sophisticated DeFi protocols (like lending and staking), the network effectively transforms Bitcoin from a passive asset into a programmable financial instrument.</p>
<p style="text-align: center;"><a class="btn btn-default" href="https://newsbtc.care/box_7271b6427956901b28f9e1ee77c086e1" rel="noopener nofollow" target="_blank">VISIT THE OFFICIAL $HYPER PRESALE SITE</a></p>
<h2>Whale Accumulation Signals Confidence In Hyper’s $31M Presale</h2>
<p>Traders often watch &#8216;smart money&#8217; wallet movements to gauge a project&#8217;s viability before the public launch. On-chain metrics for Bitcoin Hyper suggest real interest from high-net-worth individuals positioning themselves ahead of the Token Generation Event (TGE).</p>
<p>According to the official presale page, $HYPER has already raised over $31M, a figure that underscores strong demand for Bitcoin-native DeFi solutions. With tokens currently priced at $0.0136754, the valuation reflects an early-entry opportunity relative to established L2s like Stacks or fast-execution chains like Solana.</p>
<p>But even more telling is the behavior of large-volume buyers. Whales have been appearing in pods, with large purchases totalling over $1M; the largest of these was <a href="https://newsbtc.care/box_7271b6427956901b28f9e1ee77c086e1" rel="noopener nofollow" target="_blank"><strong>$500K</strong></a>. This specific accumulation during a presale phase implies a long-term conviction in the project&#8217;s roadmap and its high-APY staking incentives, which are designed to reward community governance.</p>
<p>The combination of significant capital raises and whale activity suggests the market views this SVM-integration model not just as a technical upgrade, but as a necessary evolution for the Bitcoin ecosystem.</p>

newsbtc_1770735612000_334011|1770735612000|2026|2|7|2026-02-10|newsbtc|Bernstein Calls Bitcoin Crash A ‘Crisis Of Confidence,’ Maintains $150,000 Target|<p>Despite a sharp decline in Bitcoin (BTC) prices since last October, analysts at Bernstein argue that the current downturn does not resemble a traditional crypto bear market. </p>
<p>In a <a href="https://economictimes.indiatimes.com/news/international/us/btc-usd-price-prediction-bernstein-breaks-down-why-recent-bitcoin-crash-is-weakest-bear-case-in-history-and-predicts-crypto-will-hit-150000-in-2026/articleshow/128119959.cms?from=mdr" rel="noopener nofollow" target="_blank">note </a>to clients released on Monday, the firm described the pullback as “the weakest Bitcoin bear case in its history,” even as the asset has fallen about 44% from its all‑time highs in current trading.</p>
<h2>Bernstein Defends Bitcoin’s Fundamentals</h2>
<p>The analysis was led by Bernstein’s Gautam Chhugani, who said the recent sell‑off reflects a loss of confidence rather than deeper structural problems. </p>
<p>The analysts emphasized that Bitcoin’s core fundamentals remain intact and that the decline should not be mistaken for a systemic breakdown. Bernstein reaffirmed its long‑term outlook, maintaining a $150,000 price target for Bitcoin by the end of 2026.</p>

<p>Bernstein noted that many of the “red flags” that have historically preceded major Bitcoin crashes are missing this time. The analyst asserts that there have been no large <a href="https://www.newsbtc.com/breaking-news-ticker/bitcoin-crashes-below-67000-as-stifel-warns-of-potential-drop-to-38000/" rel="noopener " target="_blank">institutional collapses</a>, no exposure of hidden leverage, and no widespread failures across the crypto ecosystem. </p>
<p>Instead, the firm sees a market weighed down by negative sentiment, even as broader conditions appear unusually favorable. The analysts pointed to what they described as strong institutional support for Bitcoin. </p>
<p>This includes a pro‑Bitcoin US president, the continued expansion of spot Bitcoin <a href="https://www.newsbtc.com/bitcoin-news/bitcoin-crash-exposes-colossal-corporate-losses-heres-whos-most-impacted/" rel="noopener " target="_blank">exchange‑traded funds</a> (ETFs), growing adoption by corporate treasuries, and sustained interest from large asset managers. </p>
<p>In Bernstein’s view, these factors clearly distinguish the current cycle from past downturns that were driven by excess risk and fragile market structures.</p>
<h2>Holders And Miners Can Weather Long Downturn</h2>
<p>The firm also addressed shifting narratives around technology trends. Bernstein noted that some investors now argue Bitcoin has become irrelevant as global attention turns toward <a href="https://www.newsbtc.com/breaking-news-ticker/expert-predicts-bitcoin-price-could-fall-to-45000-by-end-of-2026/" rel="noopener " target="_blank">artificial intelligence</a> (AI). </p>
<p>The analysts dismissed that view, saying it reflects changing investor focus rather than a genuine threat to Bitcoin’s role. They added that fears around quantum computing have similarly been overstated, pointing out that such risks would affect all critical digital systems, not just Bitcoin.</p>
<p>The firm further downplayed fears of forced selling driven by corporate treasuries or miner capitulation. Bernstein said major companies holding Bitcoin have structured their balance sheets to withstand prolonged downturns. </p>

<p>Referencing comments from Strategy’s recent <a href="https://www.newsbtc.com/bitcoin-news/bitcoin-must-fall-90-for-years-to-pressure-strategys-debt-ceo-says/" rel="noopener " target="_blank">earnings call</a>, the analysts noted that only an extreme scenario—Bitcoin falling to $8,000 and remaining there for five years—would trigger a need for restructuring.</p>
<p>Miners, they added, are also better positioned than in past cycles. Many have diversified their revenue by reallocating power resources toward AI data center demand, reducing reliance on Bitcoin mining alone and easing pressure from production costs.</p>

newsbtc_1770732004000_9431511|1770732004000|2026|2|7|2026-02-10|newsbtc|Ethereum Drops Under MVRV Band That Marked Last 3 Bottoms|<p>On-chain data shows Ethereum dipped under a key Market Value to Realized Value (MVRV) pricing band during the latest price drawdown.</p>
<h2>Ethereum Fell Under The 0.80 MVRV Band Recently</h2>
<p>As explained by analyst Ali Martinez in an X <a href="https://x.com/alicharts/status/2020530813821923751" rel="noopener nofollow" target="_blank">post</a>, Ethereum recently dropped below the 0.80 MVRV pricing band. The &#8220;<a href="https://www.newsbtc.com/xrp-news/xrp-mvrv-ratio-flashes-signal-last-630-surge/" rel="noopener " target="_blank">MVRV Ratio</a>&#8221; is a popular on-chain indicator that tracks the ratio between the ETH market cap and Realized Cap.</p>

<p>The <a href="https://www.newsbtc.com/bitcoin-news/bitcoin-lacks-fresh-momentum-realized-cap-declining/" rel="noopener " target="_blank">Realized Cap</a> here refers to a capitalization model that calculates the asset&#8217;s total value by assuming that the value of each individual token is equal to the spot price at which it was last transacted on the blockchain.</p>
<p>The last transfer of any token is likely to represent the last time that it changed hands, so the price at its time could be considered as its current cost basis. As such, the Realized Cap essentially measures the sum of the acquisition value of all coins in circulation. In other words, it provides an estimate for the amount of capital that the investors as a whole have put into the cryptocurrency.</p>
<p>As the <a href="https://www.newsbtc.com/analysis/xrp/xrp-not-reaching-10000-flawed/" rel="noopener " target="_blank">market cap</a> can be considered as the value that holders are carrying in the present, its comparison with the Realized Cap in the MVRV Ratio tells us about the profit-loss status of the Ethereum userbase.</p>
<p>When the value of the MVRV Ratio is greater than 1, it means the investors are in a state of net unrealized profit. On the other hand, it being under this mark suggests the dominance of loss on the network. Historically, profitability swinging to an extreme value either side of 1 has often paved way for reversals in the asset.</p>
<p>At a high level above 1, this happens because investors become more likely to take their profits the higher that they get. Similarly, below 1, the asset can bottom out as losses dominate and selling pressure runs out.</p>
<p>The MVRV Pricing Bands is a model that defines price levels for ETH where these behaviors become more apparent. Below is the chart shared by Martinez that shows the trend in this model&#8217;s bands for Ethereum.</p>
<img alt="Ethereum MVRV Pricing Bands" height="2700" src="https://pbs.twimg.com/media/HAoVv_RXUAAUzwR?format=jpg&amp;name=4096x4096" width="2160" />
<p>As is visible in the graph, Ethereum plunged below the 1.0 pricing band corresponding to $2,449 during its slide at the end of January. This means that the overall market went underwater due to the price drawdown.</p>
<p>With bearish momentum continuing in the first week of February, losses only grew deeper for investors as the asset fell below another pricing band: 0.80. Currently, this level is valued at $1,959.</p>

<p>&#8220;The last three times Ethereum $ETH dipped below the 0.80 Pricing Band, it marked a market bottom,&#8221; noted the analyst. It now remains to be seen whether the venture below the level would also mark a bottom for the asset this time.</p>
<h2>ETH Price</h2>
<p>Ethereum has rebounded a bit since its plunge last week as its price has returned to $2,044, recovering above the 0.80 MVRV pricing band.</p>

newsbtc_1770721256000_8530300|1770721256000|2026|2|7|2026-02-10|newsbtc|Bitcoin Bulls Hear ‘Fed–Treasury Accord’ And Smell Yield-Curve Control|<p>Kevin Warsh’s push for a new Fed–Treasury “accord” is reigniting a familiar market argument: whether Washington is drifting toward a softer-rate, higher-liquidity regime that tends to favor hard assets, including bitcoin and crypto, even if it raises the stakes for bonds.</p>
<p>The debate flared after Bloomberg reported that <a href="https://www.newsbtc.com/news/trump-nominates-crypto-kevin-warsh-for-fed-chair/" rel="noopener " target="_blank">Kevin Warsh</a> floated the idea of “a new accord with the Treasury Department,” echoing the 1951 agreement that redefined the relationship between the two institutions. Bloomberg reported over the weekend that the concept could amount to a limited bureaucratic revamp, but a more ambitious effort could “see increased volatility and concern over the US central bank&#8217;s independence,” depending on how explicitly it <a href="https://www.newsbtc.com/bitcoin-news/kevin-warsh-bitcoin-regime-shift-jeff-park/" rel="noopener " target="_blank">links the Fed’s balance sheet decisions</a> to Treasury financing.</p>
<p>Looming over the idea is the political pressure to treat debt-service costs as a policy constraint. Bloomberg pointed to interest costs “running at an annual clip of around $1 trillion,” and quoted SGH Macro Advisors’ Tim Duy warning that an accord could be read as something more than process reform. “Rather than insulating the Fed, it could look more like a framework for yield-curve control,” Duy said. “A public agreement that synchronizes the Fed’s balance sheet with Treasury financing explicitly ties monetary operations to deficits.”</p>

<h2>Can Bitcoin Get The Bid?</h2>
<p>In bitcoin circles, the accord conversation is being interpreted through the lens of yield-curve control (YCC) and debt monetization, not just the path of the policy rate. Luke Gromen framed it bluntly, citing a recent FFTT view: “Our base case is that Warsh will be as dovish as Trump needs.” He added a familiar punchline for macro traders: “Math &gt; Narratives (again).”</p>
<blockquote class="twitter-tweet">
<p dir="ltr" lang="en">“Our base case is that Warsh will be as dovish as Trump needs.” -FFTT, last week</p>
<p>Math &gt; Narratives (again) <a href="https://t.co/aHMDlz2jzM" rel="nofollow">pic.twitter.com/aHMDlz2jzM</a></p>
<p>— Luke Gromen (@LukeGromen) <a href="https://twitter.com/LukeGromen/status/2020628035050016783?ref_src=twsrc%5Etfw" rel="nofollow">February 8, 2026</a></p></blockquote>
<p>Analyst Lukas Ekwueme took the <a href="https://x.com/ekwufinance/status/2020791374971281541" rel="noopener nofollow" target="_blank">argument</a> further: “Warsh, the next Fed chair, will inflate the debt away. He is in favor of yield curve control. This means pegging US short-term interest rates to an artificially low level. The Fed commits to buying unlimited amounts above that level to push interest rates down.”</p>
<p>In that telling, the Fed pegs yields at “an artificially low level” and backs the peg with potentially unlimited purchases — a structure Ekwueme compared to the World War II era. He argued the political logic is straightforward: nominating someone “more hawkish than Powell” would clash with Trump’s prior attacks on the Fed for being too hawkish, making a dovish tilt the more consistent outcome.</p>
<p>Bull Theory, a crypto-focused account, <a href="https://x.com/BullTheoryio/status/2020802875413397774" rel="noopener nofollow" target="_blank">echoed</a> the historical parallel while stressing that Warsh’s public framing is also about reducing the Fed’s entanglement in long-duration government financing. The account argued Warsh could prefer a portfolio shift toward Treasury bills, a smaller balance sheet, and clearer limits on when large bond-buying programs can occur — potentially with “closer coordination with the Treasury on debt issuance.” But it also warned the market shouldn’t confuse “limits” with “tightening” if the end result is a policy mix that suppresses real yields and keeps liquidity conditions easy.</p>
<p>CoinFund President Christopher Perkins <a href="https://x.com/perkinscr97/status/2020654501623976099" rel="noopener nofollow" target="_blank">added</a>: “I continue to think that the crypto markets got the Warsh appointment wrong. A new Fed-Treasury Accord is the plan&#8230;has been all along. Additional coordination, or any shift in responsibilities to <a href="https://www.newsbtc.com/bitcoin-news/bitcoin-explode-bessent-250-billion-deregulation/" rel="noopener " target="_blank">Scott Bessent</a> and the US Treasury will bullish for crypto IMO&#8211;once things settle. At least for the next 3 years.”</p>

<p>For bitcoin, the central question is the direction of real yields and the credibility of the “independence” anchor because both feed into how investors price fiat debasement risk and liquidity scarcity.</p>
<p>The pro-crypto interpretation is consistent: if an accord evolves into a framework that caps parts of the curve or otherwise lowers real yields, it can push capital out the risk-free complex and into assets that behave like inflation hedges or duration substitutes. Bull Theory put it in plain terms: “If Warsh’s framework leads to lower real yields, rate cuts, and easier liquidity conditions, that usually supports risk assets like equities, gold, and crypto. Because when bond returns fall, capital looks for higher-return alternatives.”</p>
<p>The caveat is that the same setup could increase volatility in rates markets. Bloomberg flagged that an ambitious accord could spook investors about the Fed’s independence, while Bull Theory argued that reduced Fed support for long-term yields alongside heavy Treasury issuance could steepen the curve and lift term premiums.</p>
<p>For crypto traders, that combination can create a two-speed regime: supportive liquidity narratives on one hand, and sudden risk-off impulses if bond volatility spills into broader financial conditions.</p>
<p>At press time, BTC traded at $69,151.</p>

newsbtc_1770717619000_3133495|1770717619000|2026|2|7|2026-02-10|newsbtc|Ethereum Supply on Exchanges Mirrors 2016 Levels: What Happens Next?|<p>Ethereum is attempting to stabilize around the $2,000 level as the broader crypto market enters a critical consolidation phase following weeks of heightened volatility. Price action remains fragile, with buyers defending key psychological support while macro uncertainty, liquidity shifts, and persistent selling pressure continue to weigh on sentiment. Analysts note that the current environment resembles previous transitional periods where market structure weakened before a clearer directional move emerged.</p>

<p>A recent CryptoQuant report highlights an important contrast in exchange-flow dynamics between Bitcoin and Ethereum. According to the data, significant amounts of Bitcoin have recently been deposited onto exchanges, pushing exchange-held BTC supply back to levels last seen around 2019. However, a notable portion of this supply appears to belong to investors who simply custody assets on exchanges rather than actively preparing to sell, making interpretation less straightforward.</p>
<p>Ethereum presents a different picture. Despite launching in 2015 and expanding dramatically since then, the amount of ETH held on exchanges currently mirrors levels observed around mid-2016. This unusually low exchange <a href="https://www.newsbtc.com/bitcoin-news/bitcoin-short-term-holders-deep-in-loss-mvrv-signals-capitulation-phase/" rel="noopener " target="_blank">supply</a> suggests a tighter liquid float, potentially reflecting increased long-term holding, staking participation, or DeFi deployment, all of which could influence future price dynamics.</p>








<h2>Exchange Supply Tightening Signals Potential Liquidity Shift</h2>








<p>The CryptoQuant report provides additional context on Ethereum’s exchange supply dynamics by highlighting a historical comparison. In the referenced chart, the red box marks the current amount of ETH held on exchanges, while the blue box reflects a similar spot supply level last seen around mid-2016. Despite Ethereum’s substantial growth in adoption, liquidity, and institutional participation since then, exchange balances remain unusually low.</p>
<img alt="Ethereum Exchange Reserve | Source: CryptoQuant " height="720" src="https://i0.wp.com/img.cryptoquant.com/759489/quicktake/aOMaNE3Q_8d0105b087b036f962aabc348446732a80bbb37a7a8f146100e0b4328a2733ee.png?resize=1280%2C720&#038;ssl=1" width="1280" />
<p>However, because a significant portion of this ETH still belongs to investors rather than active traders, it remains uncertain whether such constrained exchange supply can persist over time. This makes ongoing monitoring of exchange inflows and outflows particularly relevant for assessing future price stability.</p>
<p>The report also notes that Ethereum’s over-the-counter (OTC) balances have increased recently. Even so, this liquidity pool remains relatively modest compared with exchange-held supply. Limiting its ability to fully offset sudden demand shocks or selling waves. If exchange balances were to tighten further while OTC liquidity also declined, the market could face sharper price reactions to incremental demand changes.</p>
<p>Such a scenario raises structural questions about market dynamics. Reduced immediately available supply could amplify volatility, intensify short squeezes, or accelerate price discovery phases, depending on broader macro sentiment and capital flows.</p>










<h2>Ethereum Tests Critical Support as Bearish Momentum Persists</h2>








<p>Ethereum continues to trade under sustained pressure after losing key support levels and briefly testing the $2,000 zone. A psychological threshold that now defines the short-term battlefield between buyers and sellers. The chart shows a clear deterioration in market structure since late 2025, with ETH consistently printing lower highs while repeatedly failing to reclaim its major moving averages. Price currently sits below the 50-, 100-, and 200-period averages, confirming a firmly bearish trend.</p>
<img alt="ETH testing key demand level | Source: ETHUSDT chart on TradingView " class="wp-image-880531 size-large" height="549" src="https://www.newsbtc.com/wp-content/uploads/2026/02/ETHUSDT_2026-02-09_07-16-37.png?w=860&#038;resize=860%2C549" width="860" />
<p>The recent breakdown accelerated as volume expanded sharply, suggesting forced selling rather than orderly repositioning. This kind of volume spike often accompanies liquidation cascades or defensive portfolio adjustments, particularly in derivatives-heavy environments. Notably, the bounce from the lows remains modest, indicating limited immediate demand absorption.</p>

<p>From a technical standpoint, the $2,000–$2,100 region now acts as fragile support. Losing it decisively could expose ETH to deeper retracement levels around $1,700 or even the $1,500 zone. Where previous consolidation occurred. Conversely, stabilization above this range would be the first signal that selling pressure is easing.</p>
<p>Momentum indicators favor caution. Until Ethereum reclaims key moving averages and establishes higher lows, the broader structure suggests continued consolidation with downside risk still present.</p>

cryptopotato_1770741227000_4381965|1770741227000|2026|2|7|2026-02-10|cryptopotato|xMoney Expands Domino’s Partnership to Greece, Powering Faster Checkout Experiences|<p class="sc-FeKFz hYlDaj"><strong>[PRESS RELEASE &#8211; Vaduz, Liechtenstein, February 9th, 2026]</strong></p>
<p><a href="https://www.xmoney.com/" rel="nofollow noopener" target="_blank">xMoney</a> ($XMN) is expanding its partnership with Domino’s, bringing its payment infrastructure to <strong>Domino’s Greece</strong> following a successful rollout in Cyprus.</p>
<p>The collaboration focuses on <strong>acquiring services</strong>, enabling Domino’s Greece to accept <strong>card payments and digital wallets</strong>, including <strong>Apple Pay and Google Pay</strong>, across both web and mobile ordering platforms.</p>
<p>At the core of the integration is xMoney’s <strong>embeddable checkout solution</strong>, designed to deliver a seamless payment experience without redirection. Customers complete their orders faster, while all sensitive payment data is securely handled by xMoney’s compliant infrastructure.</p>
<p>The expansion was announced in person at a community event hosted at <strong>SuiHub Athens</strong> – a community space established to support builders and Sui ecosystem partners – bringing together the xMoney and Sui teams, Domino’s representatives, and building on xMoney’s previously <a href="https://blog.sui.io/xmoney-xportal-wallet-mastercard/" rel="nofollow noopener" target="_blank">announced</a> work with Sui to expand real-world payment access across Europe.</p>
<blockquote><p>“Domino’s operates in a high-volume, real-time environment where speed and reliability are critical,” said Manos Tsouloufris, CTO of Daufood. “xMoney’s checkout solution supports multiple payment methods in a single, seamless flow, helping us serve customers faster at scale.”</p></blockquote>
<p>While the current implementation focuses on fiat payments, the two teams are also exploring future possibilities around digital asset payments, where network speed, user experience, and confirmation times make sense for real-world commerce.</p>
<p>The launch in Greece represents the next step in a broader European expansion, reinforcing xMoney’s role as a trusted payments partner for brands that operate at scale and its presence within the Sui ecosystem reflects a growing focus on practical, consumer-facing payment experiences built for everyday use.</p>
<blockquote><p>“When people order food, they don’t think about payments, and that’s exactly the point,” said Gregorious Siourounis, Co-Founder and CEO of xMoney. “Our role is to make checkout fast, reliable, and invisible, so brands like Domino’s can focus on their customers. Bringing this experience to Greece is a natural next step.”</p></blockquote>
<p>As xMoney expands across markets and merchant use cases, XMN supports the broader ecosystem by aligning long-term participation and infrastructure growth across the network. Designed to sit alongside xMoney’s licensed payment rails, XMN helps structure how value, incentives, and future on-chain capabilities evolve, without impacting the simplicity of everyday checkout experiences.</p>
<p>Faster checkout. Less friction.</p>
<p>Payments that deliver.</p>
<p><strong>About Domino’s</strong></p>
<p>Founded in 1960, Domino&#8217;s Pizza is the largest pizza company in the world, with a significant business in both delivery and carryout pizza. It operates a network of company-owned and independent franchise stores in the United States and more than 90 international markets.</p>
<p><strong>About xMoney</strong></p>
<p>xMoney is revolutionizing the payments landscape with strategic European licenses, delivering a seamless, secure, and forward-thinking ecosystem powered by innovative product design, cutting-edge technology, and unwavering compliance. XMN, xMoney&#8217;s newly launched token, is natively integrated into the licensed and regulated payment infrastructure &#8211; empowering merchants and consumers with lightning-fast, trustworthy transactions underpinned by full regulatory transparency. Now trading on Kraken, KuCoin, MEXC, Bitvavo, Bluefin and other exchanges, XMN is primed for broader adoption with a robust pipeline of integrations ahead.</p>

cryptopotato_1770738621000_7653892|1770738621000|2026|2|7|2026-02-10|cryptopotato|Is Cardano in Trouble? Why Whales Are Abandoning Binance|<p>Cardano has experienced a sharp decline of over 10% over the past week. It started near $0.30, but heavy selling pushed it to $0.23, forming a consolidation to $0.26. Amidst strong bearish pressure, new data suggest that major traders have exited their ADA positions.</p>
<p>Alphractal founder Joao Wedson, for one, said that Cardano&#8217;s derivatives market is going through a major shift that could affect its price momentum.</p>
<h2>Cardano Follows Solana&#8217;s Path</h2>
<p>Open interest in ADA has declined sharply from $1.6 billion to $334 million, as major players have aggressively closed their positions. However, Wedson <a href="https://x.com/joao_wedson/status/2020606697409278378">explained</a> that the more important change lies in how OI is distributed across exchanges. In 2023, Binance controlled over 80% of ADA&#8217;s open interest, while 17 other exchanges combined held less than 20%.</p>
<p>By 2026, that balance has dramatically changed as Binance now holds only 22%, and Gate.io has emerged as the new leader with 31% of the market. Wedson observed that this change is significant because a similar pattern played out with Solana.</p>
<p>During SOL&#8217;s rally from $20 to $200 in 2023-2024, Binance&#8217;s dominance in open interest increased, thereby supporting price appreciation.</p>
<p>Later, as Binance&#8217;s share declined, Solana&#8217;s momentum weakened. The same trend appears to be unfolding with Cardano, and with open interest now fragmented, the altcoin&#8217;s upside potential may be limited as the overall crypto market remains fragile.</p>
<blockquote><p>&#8220;Binance tends to be the exchange that fuels strong altcoin rallies, but only when leverage is concentrated and competition is limited.&#8221;</p></blockquote>
<h2>Long-Term Trend Remains Intact</h2>
<p>Despite the short-term market uncertainty <a href="https://cryptopotato.com/falling-knife-gemini-and-chatgpt-predict-shocking-lows-for-cardanos-ada/">gripping</a> the ADA market, pseudonymous analyst, &#8216;Crypto Patel,&#8217; <a href="https://x.com/CryptoPatel/status/2019992013345603597">believes</a> that the overall long-term structure stays bullish as long as the price does not fall below $0.13 on a weekly close.</p>
<p>On the upside, he says ADA needs to reclaim $0.44 to confirm a new uptrend. If that happens, the crypto asset could enter a new bull cycle, and long-term targets range from $1.20 to as high as over $10, similar to past cycles.</p>

cryptopotato_1770719384000_1781654|1770719384000|2026|2|7|2026-02-10|cryptopotato|Vitalik Buterin Slams ‘Fake’ DeFi, Backs ETH-Based Algo Stablecoins|<p>Ethereum co-founder Vitalik Buterin has questioned the legitimacy of popular USDC yield strategies, arguing they don’t follow the principles of true decentralized finance (DeFi).</p>
<p>His critique was in response to crypto analyst C-node, who said that most modern DeFi focuses on speculative gains instead of building genuinely decentralized infrastructure.</p>
<h2>Critique of Modern DeFi</h2>
<p>C-node <a href="https://x.com/i/status/2020566745027690550">challenged</a> the crypto industry on social media, saying there is little reason to use DeFi unless users hold long cryptocurrency positions and need financial services while keeping self-custody.</p>
<p>Buterin supported this perspective, arguing that depositing stablecoins such as USDC into lending protocols like Aave does not count as true DeFi. He dismissed such strategies, stating, “inb4 ‘muh USDC yield,’ that’s not DeFi.”</p>
<p>In his view, the underlying asset remains controlled by Circle, meaning the arrangement is fundamentally centralized even if the protocol itself is decentralized.</p>
<p>The Ethereum developer <a href="https://x.com/i/status/2020595540791087517">suggested</a> two frameworks for evaluating what should qualify as real DeFi. The first, which he described as the “easy mode,” centers on ETH-backed algorithmic stablecoins. In this model, users can shift counterparty risk to market makers through collateralized debt positions (CDPs), where assets are locked to mint stablecoins.</p>
<p>He explained that even if 99% of the liquidity is backed by CDP holders who hold negative algorithmic dollars while holding positive ones elsewhere, the ability to offload counterparty risk to a market maker remains an important feature.</p>
<p>The second, or “hard mode,” framework allows for real-world asset (RWA) backing, but only under strict conditions. Buterin said an algorithmic stablecoin backed by RWAs could still qualify as DeFi if it is sufficiently overcollateralized and diversified to survive the failure of any single backing asset.</p>
<p>Under this structure, the overcollateralization ratio must be more than the maximum share of any individual asset, ensuring the system remains solvent even if one part collapses. This means that it would act as a buffer that distributes risk instead of concentrating it within centralized entities.</p>
<p>“I feel like that sort of thing is what we should be aiming more towards,” Buterin said, adding that the long-term goal should be moving away from the dollar as the unit of account toward a more diversified index.</p>
<h2>Crypto Community Response</h2>
<p>The remarks were widely supported within the X crypto community, with one user <a href="https://x.com/i/status/2020689791772418233">calling</a> it a “great take” and noting that ETH-backed algorithmic stablecoins offer real risk reduction, while RWA diversification spreads it instead of eliminating it. Another commented that &#8220;True DeFi needs real risk innovation, not just USDC parking.”</p>
<p>However, there were also some concerns. For instance, X user Kyle DH pointed out that algorithmic stablecoins have not updated their designs to address known issues, which makes them similar to money market funds that have the same “breaking the buck” risks <a href="https://cryptopotato.com/luna-collapses-below-16-as-terrausd-remains-unpegged/">seen</a> before with TerraUSD and LUNA. They added that RWA backing requires careful diversification, warning that highly correlated assets or black swan events could still cause a stablecoin to fail.</p>

cryptopotato_1770698199000_1370398|1770698199000|2026|2|7|2026-02-09|cryptopotato|How 2 Wallet Errors and Phishing Attacks Cost Crypto Users $62M|<p>In January, a crypto user lost $12.25 million by copying the wrong wallet address. In December as well, another one ended up losing $50 million in a similar way.</p>
<p>Together, the two incidents cost $62 million, according to the popular Web3 security solution, Scam Sniffer.</p>
<h2>Crypto Blunders</h2>
<p>Signature phishing attacks also surged in January. In fact, Scam Sniffer <a href="https://x.com/realScamSniffer/status/2020343088523407836">found</a> that $6.27 million was stolen from 4,741 victims, which is a 207% increase from December. The largest cases involved $3.02 million from SLVon and XAUt via permit/increaseAllowance, and $1.08 million from aEthLBTC via permit.</p>
<p>Two wallets alone accounted for 65% of all phishing losses.</p>
<p>Address poisoning is a scam where attackers send small transactions from wallet addresses that closely resemble real ones, hoping users copy the wrong address from their transaction history. This can lead to funds being sent directly to scammers by mistake. Signature phishing further increases the risk by tricking users into signing malicious approvals that give attackers permission to move funds later. As such, these tactics rely on social engineering and human error, and may make even experienced users vulnerable.</p>
<p>In November last year, a crypto holder lost over $3 million worth of PYTH tokens after mistakenly sending funds to a scammer&#8217;s wallet. The error occurred when the victim copied a fake deposit address from their transaction history.</p>
<p>Blockchain analysts at Lookonchain <a href="https://cryptopotato.com/careless-crypto-transfer-costs-investor-3-08m-details/">said</a> the attacker created a lookalike address matching the first four characters of the real wallet and sent a tiny SOL transaction to appear legitimate. The victim later transferred 7 million PYTH tokens without fully verifying the address and fell victim to an address poisoning attack. The transferred stash was worth about $3.08 million at that time.</p>
<h2>Coordinated Multisig Scam Attempt</h2>
<p>Amidst the growing frequency of such attacks, the non-custodial wallet, Safe, formerly known as Gnosis Safe, also <a href="https://x.com/SafeLabs_/status/2019709903946879149">issued</a> a warning for its users about a large-scale address poisoning and social engineering campaign targeting multisig wallets. According to the platform, attackers created thousands of lookalike Safe addresses to trick users into sending funds to the wrong destination. It disclosed that the incident was not a protocol exploit, infrastructure breach, or smart contract vulnerability.</p>
<p>Safe identified around 5,000 malicious addresses, which have now been flagged and removed from the Safe Wallet interface to reduce the risk of accidental fund transfers.</p>

On February 5, their daily inflows topped 1,000 BTC, far above the monthly average of around 365 BTC. <h2>Whales Accumulate as Price Steadies Near $70,000</h2>
<p>While miners and smaller holders sent coins to exchanges, large holders took the opposite approach. <p>Price action since then reflects that tug-of-war, with Bitcoin now trading at just over $70,000 per CoinGecko, a figure that is up about 1% on the day but still down nearly 8% over the past week and more than 22% in the last 30 days. The rebound followed a sharp fall from the mid-$80,000 range, part of a broader slide that <a href="https://cryptopotato.com/bitcoin-erases-post-trump-election-gains-altcoins-crash-by-double-digits-your-weekly-crypto-recap/">erased</a> gains made after the U.S. election and dragged major altcoins down by double digits.</p>

As things stand, elevated miner inflows point to ongoing supply hitting the market, while whale accumulation and reduced retail selling suggest that selling pressure is no longer one-sided, with BTC attempting to hold above $70,000.</p>

<h2>Bitcoin is Better Than Gold</h2>
<p>According to Kiyosaki, investing in both gold and bitcoin, and adding silver, will be appropriate for capital diversification. However, when asked to choose one asset, he would go for bitcoin. This is because gold is infinite in theory, while BTC is finite by design.</p>
<p>As the value of metal rises, more gold miners will dig for more, and this could increase the amount of the bullion in circulation. Bitcoin, on the other hand, is designed to have a limit of 21 million units.</p>
<p>The asset has a current circulating supply of 19.98 million, less than 2 million BTC away from reaching the limit. This means no more BTC can be added to circulation after the network mines 21 million units, ensuring long-term scarcity. Kiyosaki called this a brilliant strategy that could propel the value of BTC upwards.</p>
<blockquote><p>“Glad I bought my Bitcoin early. I am still actively mining for gold and drilling for oil,” the author added.</p></blockquote>

<p>The divergence between falling prices and rising network activity is often associated with panic-driven behavior, where holders rush to move assets during fast drawdowns.</p>
<p>CryptoOnchain linked the spike to investors rotating into stablecoins, moving funds onto exchanges for sale, and a wave of liquidations across decentralized finance protocols as collateral values fell.</p>
<blockquote><p>“This significant spike in ERC-20 token transfers during a price crash suggests investors are rushing to exit positions, likely converting volatile assets into stablecoins or moving funds to exchanges for liquidation,” the market observer wrote.</p></blockquote>
<p>The timing also lines up with a broader market sell-off that saw Bitcoin fall from above $80,000 to near $60,000 before rebounding toward $72,000, while Ethereum struggled to hold key support near $2,000.</p>

<p>On the other hand, falling exchange balances suggest fewer coins are readily available for spot selling, and some of the recent transfers may reflect stress-driven repositioning rather than long-term distribution. According to CryptoOnchain, similar spikes in transfer activity during past drawdowns have sometimes occurred near local lows, once forced selling eased.</p>
<p>For now, Ethereum sits between ongoing volatility and shrinking exchange supply, with on-chain data showing fear-driven movement even as longer-term holders continue pulling coins off trading platforms.</p>
