cryptopotato_1770677188000_5319941|1770677188000|2026|2|7|2026-02-09|cryptopotato|Important Binance Announcement Concerning Ripple (XRP) And Other Altcoin Traders: Details Here|<p>The world&#8217;s largest crypto exchange will implement certain amendments to address ongoing market trends and enhance the trading experience for users.</p>
<p>Some of the cryptocurrencies included in the upcoming efforts are Ripple (XRP), Sui (SUI), Aster (ASTER), Internet Computer (ICP), and others.</p>
<h2>The New Additions</h2>
<p>The company <a href="https://www.binance.com/en/support/announcement/detail/a79548cf58c34b779731403610c7e7bb">announced</a> it will expand the list of trading pairs on Binance Spot by adding XRP/U, SUI/U, ASTER/U, and PAXG/U. The listing is scheduled for February 10, whereas trading bots services for the aforementioned pairs will become available on the same date.</p>
<p>U stands for United Stables &#8211; a stablecoin launched toward the end of 2025 and pegged to the US dollar. Binance revealed that all eligible users will enjoy zero maker fees on XRP/U, SUI/U, and ASTER/U &#8220;until further notice.&#8221; In addition, VIP clients will be offered zero-taker fees on those pairs.</p>
<p>The exchange informed that the new offerings will not be available to all users, noting that those residing in the USA, Canada, Iran, the Netherlands, and other countries will be excluded.</p>
<p>While backing from Binance may be price-positive for the included cryptocurrencies, such an effect is generally observed at initial listings rather than from the addition of extra trading pairs. In fact, XRP, SUI, and ASTER have headed south today (February 9), coinciding with the overall decline of the broader crypto market.</p>
<h2>Goodbye to These Pairs</h2>
<p>Besides adding new offerings, Binance regularly monitors its service offerings and removes pairs that don&#8217;t meet the required criteria. Recently, it <a href="https://www.binance.com/en/support/announcement/detail/fa494850a7a34b4ebdc6e55beb40f63f">announced</a> it will scrap 20 pairs, including BERA/BTC, ICP/ETH, KAITO/FDUSD, MANA/ETH, ZRO/BTC, and others.</p>
<blockquote>
<p class=" richtext-paragraph css-zwb0rk"><span class="richtext-text css-83xnqe">&#8220;The delisting of a spot trading pair does </span><span class="richtext-text css-83xnqe">not</span><span class="richtext-text css-83xnqe"> affect the availability of the tokens on Binance Spot. Users can still trade the spot trading pair&#8217;s base and quote assets on other trading pair(s) that are available on Binance,&#8221; the company clarified.</span></p>
</blockquote>

cryptopotato_1770671195000_6712495|1770671195000|2026|2|7|2026-02-09|cryptopotato|CryptoGames Advances Transparency and Mathematical Fairness in iGaming|<p class="sc-FeKFz hYlDaj"><strong>[PRESS RELEASE &#8211; Willemstad, Curaçao, February 9th, 2026]</strong></p>
<p>CryptoGames announced that players on its platform have placed over 9.5 billion Dice bets, marking a notable usage milestone and reflecting consistent engagement with its provably fair gaming system. The volume of verified wagers underscores the platform’s ongoing focus on transparency, statistical fairness, and game integrity.</p>
<p>Founded in 2020, <a href="https://crypto.games/" rel="nofollow noopener" target="_blank">CryptoGames</a> was built around a clear guiding principle: to offer a gambling environment where fairness can be independently verified, odds are fully understood, and competition takes place on equal terms. Rather than relying on large libraries of third-party games with opaque mechanics, CryptoGames delivers a focused portfolio of internally developed titles, each engineered with some of the lowest house edges available online.</p>
<p><strong>House Edge as a Foundation of Long-Term Value</strong></p>
<p>In gambling mathematics, house edge defines the casino’s statistical advantage over time. While short-term outcomes can vary, long-term results are shaped almost entirely by this single metric. Even small differences in house edge can have a measurable impact when applied across a high volume of bets.</p>
<p>CryptoGames emphasizes transparency in house edge as a core aspect of its platform design. The platform offers low-margin games, which may result in higher value retention for players over extended periods of play, compared to traditional online casinos where house edges typically range from 4% to 10%.</p>
<p><strong>In-House Development Enables Competitive Margins</strong></p>
<p>All games on CryptoGames are developed internally. This approach removes the need for third-party licensing fees and external profit margins, allowing the platform to operate efficiently while offering leaner house edges.</p>
<p><strong>Standard House Edge Across Games</strong></p>
<p>CryptoGames maintains consistent and competitive margins across its game selection:</p>
<ul>
<li>Dice – 1.0%</li>
<li>DiceV2 – 1.0%</li>
<li>Keno – 1.0%</li>
<li>Minesweeper – 1.0%</li>
<li>Blackjack – 1.25%</li>
<li>Roulette – 2.7%</li>
<li>Plinko – 1.72%</li>
<li>Slot – 1.97%</li>
</ul>
<p>The Lottery game stands out with a 0.0% house edge, an uncommon structure that reinforces CryptoGames’ commitment to fairness and transparency.</p>
<p>By comparison, these margins offer players a measurable advantage over conventional casino offerings over time.</p>
<p><strong>Provably Fair Technology Built Into Every Bet</strong></p>
<p>Transparency is reinforced through full implementation of provably fair gaming across the CryptoGames platform.</p>
<p>Before each wager, the server seed is hashed and presented to the player. Once the bet concludes, the original seed is revealed, allowing independent verification of the outcome using the published algorithm.</p>
<p>By design, this eliminates one of the most common trust concerns in online gambling.</p>
<p><strong>Broad Cryptocurrency Support and Flexible Access</strong></p>
<p><a href="https://crypto.games/" rel="nofollow noopener" target="_blank">CryptoGames</a> supports betting with 14 cryptocurrencies, accommodating a wide range of blockchain users.</p>
<p>Through ChangeNow integration, users can also deposit more than 50 additional altcoins, which are automatically converted into supported assets. For those new to crypto, CryptoGames integrates the Swapped fiat-to-crypto gateway, enabling purchases via credit cards, Apple Pay, and Google Pay.</p>
<p><strong>Ongoing Rewards Designed for Consistent Engagement</strong></p>
<p>CryptoGames emphasizes long-term engagement through recurring rewards rather than one-time promotional offers.</p>
<p><strong>Monthly Wagering Contest With Major Prize Pools</strong></p>
<p>The platform hosts a monthly wagering contest offering rewards of up to $500,000 USD, depending on market conditions.</p>
<p>Leaderboards are separated by cryptocurrency, ensuring fair competition among players using the same assets. Participants also receive lottery tickets throughout the month, adding additional reward opportunities tied to consistent participation.</p>
<p><strong>VIP Program Focused on Statistical Advantage</strong></p>
<p>CryptoGames’ VIP program is tailored for high-volume and competitive players.</p>
<p><strong>VIP Benefits</strong></p>
<ul>
<li>Reduced dice house edge of 0.8%</li>
<li>Removal of server-side betting delays</li>
<li>Increased daily exchange limits up to 1 BTC</li>
<li>Access to a private VIP chat room</li>
<li>VIP chat identification</li>
<li>$100 Bitcoin birthday bonus (Tier 3 KYC required)</li>
<li>Additional faucet level</li>
<li>Monthly voucher distributions</li>
</ul>
<p>Players who maintain VIP status for three consecutive months retain most benefits even if they do not immediately requalify, reinforcing long-term loyalty.</p>
<p><strong>Optimized User Experience and Community Engagement</strong></p>
<p>CryptoGames delivers a clean, high-performance interface designed for speed and efficiency. Betting remains smooth even at high volumes. An active chatbox, blog, and forum further support transparency and community interaction.</p>
<p><strong>A Platform Built for Fairness, Strategy, and Confidence</strong></p>
<p>With more than 9.5 billion Dice bets placed, <a href="https://crypto.games/" rel="nofollow noopener" target="_blank">CryptoGames</a> continues to demonstrate the scalability and reliability of its provably fair systems. Through in-house development, transparent odds, extensive crypto support, and competitive reward structures, CryptoGames sets a disciplined standard in the crypto gambling space.</p>
<p>For users focused on long-term value, verifiable fairness, and confident decision-making, CryptoGames represents a clear and data-driven approach to crypto gaming.</p>
<p><strong>About CryptoGames</strong></p>
<p>CryptoGames is a cryptocurrency-focused iGaming platform founded in 2020, built around the principles of transparency, mathematical fairness, and player-verifiable outcomes. The platform offers a curated selection of internally developed games with consistently low house edges, supported by provably fair technology that allows every wager to be independently verified. By combining in-house development, broad cryptocurrency support, and data-driven game design, CryptoGames provides a gambling environment designed for informed decision-making and long-term value.</p>

<p>Several months later, he tried a really risky bet. He <a href="https://cryptopotato.com/heres-how-much-bitcoin-btc-drake-lost-after-argentina-qualified-for-copa-americas-final/">wagered</a> $300,000 in the primary cryptocurrency on Canada&#8217;s national football team to win against the reigning world champion Argentina. The odds for the North American country were almost 10, meaning Drake would have made a substantial profit. Somewhat expectedly, however, the team captained by Lionel Messi won by 2-0.</p>
<p>Those losses (and many more) over the years gave rise to the so-called &#8220;Drake curse.&#8221; It is a popular Internet meme that refers to the pattern where the rapper publicly supports or bets on a club or athlete, only for them to lose in the aftermath.</p>

<h2>Bitcoin Price Analysis: The Daily Chart</h2>
<p>On the daily timeframe, Bitcoin remains structurally bearish, as the price has been printing major lower highs and has reached the channel’s lower boundary. <p>However, once the asset reached the $60K–$62K demand zone, selling pressure decelerated sharply. Since tapping this zone, Bitcoin has managed to recover toward the $69K–$70K region, but the rebound has lacked momentum and follow-through.</p>
<p>The daily chart now reflects balance rather than trend. Sellers are no longer pressing prices lower aggressively, yet buyers are also unable to reclaim the former support at $75K–$77K, which has now transitioned into a clear supply zone. As long as Bitcoin remains capped below that area, the broader daily bias stays cautious, with consolidation favored over continuation.</p>

<p>Zooming into the 4-hour timeframe, it is evident that the price has rebounded from the $60K threshold, and is now oscillating around $69K–$70K. The character of price action has shifted from impulsive candles to overlapping ranges, signaling exhaustion on the sell side.</p>
<p>The channel’s mid trendline is considered the main supply range near the $73K area, while the internal resistance around the $70K consistently rejects upside attempts. On the downside, demand remains clearly defined between $60K and $62K, where buyers previously stepped in with conviction.</p>
<p>This creates a compressed environment where Bitcoin is effectively boxed between a rising demand floor and a descending resistance ceiling. <p><a href="https://cryptopotato.com/wp-content/uploads/2026/02/BTC-4H-3-scaled.jpg"><img alt="" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-1428279" height="1481" src="https://cryptopotato.com/wp-content/uploads/2026/02/BTC-4H-3-scaled.jpg" width="2560" /></a></p>
<h2>Sentiment Analysis</h2>
<p>Bitcoin has now reached the realized price of the 18-month to 2-year holder cohort, placing this group in a breakeven state. This level, located around the $60K range, is particularly important because it often acts as a behavioral inflection point, where holders are more likely to either defend their cost basis or exit positions if confidence weakens.</p>
<p>From an on-chain perspective, this realized price currently functions as a key support zone. If buying pressure absorbs supply at this level, the market is likely to stabilize and transition into a consolidation phase. However, failure to hold this area could trigger additional sell pressure as this cohort moves into a loss.</p>
<p>On the upside, the realized price of the 12-month to 18-month cohort around $85K-$90K now represents a clear resistance, as these holders are underwater and may sell into any relief rally. Overall, Bitcoin is trading at a critical equilibrium zone where consolidation is favored unless a decisive break occurs in either direction.</p>

<h2>Takaichi’s Victory Reshapes Capital Flows</h2>
<p>Market reaction to the election was swift, with Japanese stocks pushed to fresh record highs in the hours after the result, and the Nikkei extending gains as traders priced in aggressive fiscal stimulus and a more tolerant stance toward yen weakness.</p>
<p>Market watcher Ash Crypto <a href="https://x.com/AshCrypto/status/2020737358946242864?s=20">wrote</a> on X that Japan’s stock market had hit a new all-time high following Takaichi’s victory, reflecting optimism around domestic reflation.</p>
<p>Research firms and analysts were more cautious about global spillovers. XWIN Research <a href="https://cryptoquant.com/insights/quicktake/69890755312550148f4eae62-Landslide-Lower-House-Victory-and-the-Takaichi-Trade-Short-Term-Headwinds-and-Me">described</a> the outcome as bearish for Bitcoin in the near term, pointing to tighter global liquidity and shifting capital flows.</p>
<p>Meanwhile, GugaOnChain <a href="https://cryptoquant.com/insights/quicktake/6988cf4cc876a02133a03672-The-victory-of-the-Takaichi-Trade-Japanese-stimulus-threatens-the-momentum-of-US">noted</a> that the so-called “Takaichi Trade” is not a simple exit from U.S. assets but a portfolio rebalance. Japanese Government Bonds, sidelined for years by ultra-low yields, are attracting incremental capital as fiscal expansion raises reflation expectations.</p>
<p>That rotation has coincided with a pullback in U.S. equities. Over the past seven days, the Nasdaq Composite fell about 5.6%, the S&amp;P 500 slipped by about 2.7%, and the Russell 2000 dropped close to 2.6%.</p>
<p>A stronger dollar, driven by yen weakness and persistent rate gaps between the U.S. and Japan, has tightened financial conditions further. In these risk-off phases, Bitcoin has tended to move alongside U.S. equities, allowing equity-led de-risking to spill into crypto markets.</p>
<blockquote><p>“The Takaichi Trade strengthens Japan but puts pressure on the U.S. and Bitcoin,” wrote GugaOnChain. “The capital flight to JGBs and a robust dollar create an environment of inevitable adjustments, requiring investors to closely monitor the correlation between U.S. indexes and crypto assets.”</p></blockquote>
<h2>Weak Sentiment Now, Policy Tailwinds Later</h2>
<p>At the time of writing, BTC was trading just below $71,000, up about 2% on the day but down more than 6% over the past week and nearly 22% in the last month.</p>
<p>Adding to the feeling of fragility in the market, the Bitcoin Fear and Greed Index <a href="https://cryptopotato.com/bitcoin-fear-and-greed-index-plummets-to-6-year-low-is-the-worst-over/">fell</a> to a 6-year low on February 7 after BTC slid from above $90,000 in late January to near $60,000 before rebounding.</p>
<p>CryptoQuant’s latest report <a href="https://cryptopotato.com/cryptoquant-breaks-down-current-bear-market-signals/">shows</a> Bitcoin trading below its 365-day moving average, with spot and institutional demand weak and liquidity tightening, all common features of a bear phase.</p>
<p>Still, Japan’s political backdrop looks different beyond the immediate risk-off trade. With a two-thirds majority, Takaichi’s administration has room to pursue legislative changes, and officials have previously framed Web3 as an industrial policy focus. As such, analysts expect discussions around crypto tax reform and stablecoin rules to resume.</p>

<blockquote><p>“Near-term pressure on U.S. equities and Bitcoin is macro-driven, while Japan’s institutional reforms may support crypto markets longer term.”</p></blockquote>

The most important observation on the chart is the clean breakdown below multiple prior support levels, followed by a sharp impulsive leg to the downside. This move confirms strong bearish acceptance rather than a simple liquidity sweep.</p>
<p>The asset has now reached a major higher-timeframe demand zone, located around the $1.8K region, which previously acted as a base during earlier accumulation phases. The reaction off this zone has produced a modest bounce, but so far this move lacks structural strength and remains corrective in nature.</p>
<p>Nevertheless, the market is likely to enter a consolidation-correction phase above this crucial support until a decisive breakout occurs. The main supply zone during this consolidation range is the channel’s middle line, located at the $2.3K threshold. A break above this resistance will open the door for an extended bullish retracement toward the $2.5K significant resistance.</p>
<p><a href="https://cryptopotato.com/wp-content/uploads/2026/02/ETH-D-2-scaled.jpg"><img alt="" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-1428214" height="1481" src="https://cryptopotato.com/wp-content/uploads/2026/02/ETH-D-2-scaled.jpg" width="2560" /></a></p>
<h2>ETH/USDT 4-Hour Chart</h2>
<p>Zooming into the 4-hour timeframe, the bearish structure becomes even clearer. The most recent price action shows a sharp sell-off into demand, followed by a shallow bounce that lacks impulsive follow-through.</p>
<p>Crucially, the rebound appears corrective and technically opens the door for a pullback toward the most recent supply zones and Fibonacci levels, located around the $2.3K to $2.6K region. These areas align with prior breakdown levels and correspond to zones where sellers previously intervened aggressively. If the price retraces into these levels without strong volume or momentum, they are likely to act as rejection zones rather than breakout points.</p>
<p>Until Ethereum can reclaim and hold above these supply areas, the 4-hour structure continues to favour continuation to the downside or extended consolidation within the lower range, rather than a trend reversal.</p>
<p><a href="https://cryptopotato.com/wp-content/uploads/2026/02/ETH-4H-3-scaled.jpg"><img alt="" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-1428213" height="1481" src="https://cryptopotato.com/wp-content/uploads/2026/02/ETH-4H-3-scaled.jpg" width="2560" /></a></p>
<h2>Sentiment Analysis</h2>
<p>The ETH liquidation heatmap over the last 6 months provides critical confirmation of the bearish technical structure. A significant concentration of liquidity has been built around and just below the $2K level, which has recently acted as a strong magnet for price. The sharp sell-off into this area confirms that downside liquidity was actively targeted, resulting in a large flush of leveraged long positions.</p>
<p>Despite this liquidation event, the heatmap still reveals residual liquidity pockets extending slightly below current price levels, indicating that the market may not have fully exhausted its downside objectives yet. These remaining clusters continue to exert gravitational pull on price, especially if spot demand remains weak and derivatives positioning rebuilds on the long side too quickly.</p>
<p>That said, the intensity of liquidations around the $2K zone suggests that a meaningful portion of forced selling has already occurred. This reduces immediate liquidation pressure and explains the short-term stabilization seen after the drop. However, from an on-chain perspective, this behavior supports consolidation or corrective rebounds, not a confirmed trend reversal, unless liquidity interest decisively shifts back above current levels.</p>
<p>In summary, on-chain data aligns closely with the technical picture: Ethereum is still operating in a bearish liquidity-driven environment, with downside risks remaining active as long as price fails to reclaim key supply zones and attract sustained spot demand.</p>

cryptopotato_1770600499000_6543553|1770600499000|2026|2|6|2026-02-08|cryptopotato|South Korea Jails Crypto CEO in First-Ever Case Under New Virtual Asset Law|<p>A South Korean court has sentenced Jong-hwan Lee, CEO of a local crypto asset management firm, to three years in prison for manipulating cryptocurrency prices to secure illicit profits.</p>
<p>The Seoul Southern District Court ruled on Wednesday that Lee violated the Virtual Asset User Protection Act, earning approximately 7.1 billion Korean won (which is worth around $4.88 million) through price manipulation.</p>
<h2>Court Findings</h2>
<p>In addition to the prison term, the court imposed a fine of 500 million won, nearly $344,000, and ordered the forfeiture of around 846 million won, or $581,900 in criminal proceeds. However, Lee was not taken into custody during the court proceedings, as the judges cited his good behavior throughout the trial.</p>
<p>The court <a href="https://www.hankyung.com/article/2026020443831">found</a> that between July 22 and October 25, 2024, Lee employed an automated trading program to inflate trading volumes and repeatedly place wash trades in the ACE cryptocurrency. Investigators reported that the daily trading volume of ACE jumped from roughly 160,000 units to 2.45 million units overnight, and Lee was responsible for 89% of the activity.</p>
<p>Min-cheol Kang, a former employee of the firm also indicted in the case, received a two-year prison sentence with three years of probation. While the court confirmed the defendants&#8217; involvement in manipulating ACE for unfair profits, it partially acquitted them regarding the exact 7.1 billion won figure due to insufficient evidence.</p>
<p>Interestingly, this case is the first enforcement under South Korea’s Virtual Asset User Protection Act, which came into effect in July 2024.</p>
<h2>South Korea Crypto Mishap</h2>
<p>As courts move to punish crypto market abuse, other branches of the legal system are grappling with the risks tied to handling digital assets. In January, South Korean prosecutors were <a href="https://cryptopotato.com/47m-bitcoin-vanishes-from-south-korean-prosecutors-custody-in-shocking-seizure-mishap/">investigating</a> the disappearance of a large amount of Bitcoin that had been seized and stored as part of a criminal case.</p>
<p>The issue was discovered during a routine internal inspection at the Gwangju District Prosecutors’ Office, where officials check access details for confiscated assets, including credentials stored on removable devices like USB drives. While authorities have not confirmed the exact amount lost, local media estimates the missing Bitcoin could be worth around 70 billion won, or roughly $47.7 million.</p>
<p>According to officials cited in local reports, the loss may have occurred after an agency worker accessed a fraudulent website, which raised suspicion of a phishing attack rather than a direct breach of government systems. It is believed that wallet passwords or access credentials may have been exposed, allowing attackers to drain the seized funds.</p>

The company&#8217;s total cost basis for these holdings is $54.26 billion, which translates to an average cost of $76,052 per bitcoin.</p>
<p>With Bitcoin dropping to almost $60,000, well below Strategy&#8217;s average purchase price, the firm&#8217;s vast BTC treasury is currently underwater.</p>
<h2>Treasury Under Strain</h2>
<p>In 2025, Strategy <a href="https://www.strategy.com/press/strategy-announces-fourth-quarter-2025-financial-results_02-05-2026">achieved</a> a full-year BTC yield of 22.8% and recorded gains of 101,873 BTC. The company continued to expand its BTC treasury in January 2026 and ended up acquiring an additional 41,002 BTC.</p>
<p>Strategy started in 1989 as a traditional software company focused on data analytics. In 2020, co-founder Michael Saylor made a major pivot to Bitcoin, seeing it as a safer alternative to cash during pandemic-era stimulus and low interest rates. The company began using BTC as a long-term treasury asset.</p>
<p>By 2025, it rebranded as Strategy and fully embraced its role as a BTC-first company. The pivot drew attention from regulators and index providers, who questioned whether a firm dominated by crypto should remain in major indices. MSCI suggested companies holding more than half their assets in Bitcoin might be considered non-operating. Strategy, however, argued that it actively uses Bitcoin to raise capital and drive shareholder value. Attempts to join the S&amp;P 500 in September and December 2025 also failed.</p>
<p>Despite this, Strategy&#8217;s Bitcoin holdings have remained central to its financial structure and are closely tied to its digital credit instruments, particularly STRC, which acts as a complementary tool for risk management and capital amplification. STRC&#8217;s growth to $3.4 billion has been supported by higher liquidity and lower volatility in the crypto markets.</p>
<p>The company raised $25.3 billion in 2025 to support its BTC treasury and preferred stock offerings, which made it the largest US equity issuer for the second consecutive year. It also maintains a $2.25 billion USD Reserve, covering over 2.5 years of preferred stock dividends and interest obligations, providing additional stability amid market swings.</p>
<p>The recent dip in the leading crypto asset has renewed concerns about corporate BTC exposure. Popular investor Michael Burry recently <a href="https://cryptopotato.com/michael-burry-warns-bitcoin-treasury-firms-face-existential-risk-as-btc-slide-deepens/">claimed</a> that Bitcoin&#8217;s behavior as a speculative asset, rather than a hedge, could pose significant risks for companies holding large BTC treasuries. He observed that further price declines could leave major holders, including Strategy, deeply underwater and potentially limit access to capital markets, thereby amplifying financial stress.</p>
<h2>Losses Surge in Q4</h2>
<p>Meanwhile, Strategy&#8217;s operating losses for the quarter were found to be $17.4 billion, entirely due to unrealized losses on digital assets, compared with a $1.0 billion operating loss in Q4 2024 under the prior accounting model.</p>
<p>Net loss for the quarter was $12.4 billion, up from $670.8 million in the same period of 2024. Cash and cash equivalents rose to $2.3 billion from $38.1 million, driven largely by the establishment of the USD Reserve.</p>

cryptopotato_1770576709000_3539197|1770576709000|2026|2|6|2026-02-08|cryptopotato|INVESTING YACHTS Launches RWA Yacht Charter Model|<p class="sc-FeKFz hYlDaj"><strong>[PRESS RELEASE &#8211; Ibiza, Spain, February 8th, 2026]</strong></p>
<p><a href="https://investingyachts.com/" rel="nofollow noopener" target="_blank">Investing Yachts</a> today introduced its <strong>real-world asset (RWA)</strong> yacht charter model, a blockchain-based approach designed to tokenize exposure to potential <strong>double-digit revenue generated by luxury yacht charter operations</strong> via their <strong>upcoming</strong> <strong>$YATE</strong> <strong>token</strong>. Being their ultimate goal to democratize access to all private equity sectors.</p>
<p>Positioning itself at the intersection of yachting and on-chain finance, <strong>Investing Yachts</strong> is built to <strong>remove traditional barriers</strong> associated with yacht investing—such as high minimum capital requirements, illiquidity, and operational complexity—by offering a token-based structure intended to be tradable on markets and supported by a managed charter fleet.</p>
<p><strong>How the model is designed to work</strong></p>
<p>At the core of the <strong>Investing Yachts</strong> model, the $YATE ecosystem connects charter activity to tokenholder incentives through a rules-based framework:</p>
<ul>
<li><strong>Charter profit distribution:</strong> Up to <strong>65% of annual net charter profits</strong> is intended to be distributed to tokenholders who lock $YATE into protocol “vaults,” with different lock periods associated with different maximum shares of the profit pool.</li>
<li><strong>Buyback &amp; burn:</strong> A defined portion of net profits, <strong>10%,</strong> is earmarked for buying back tokens and burning them, aiming to reduce circulating supply over time.</li>
<li><strong>Asset-tied issuance:</strong> New tokens are being minted in connection with acquiring additional yachts or other real-world assets, using a NAV-based issuance framework designed to align token supply with the underlying asset base and charter activity.</li>
</ul>
<p><strong>$YATE Token Pre-Sale</strong></p>
<p><strong>Investing Yachts</strong> states that the <strong>$YATE pre-sale is scheduled to open on February 25, 2026</strong>, with the goal of expanding community participation ahead of broader exchange availability.</p>
<p>As described on the website and in the whitepaper documentation, the pre-sale pricing is structured as follows:</p>
<ul>
<li><strong>Initial price:</strong> <strong>0.10 USDT</strong> per $YATE</li>
<li><strong>Dynamic increase:</strong> +0.75% price increase every 24 hours</li>
<li><strong>Duration:</strong> 9 months</li>
<li><strong>Target post–pre-sale listing price:</strong> <strong>1.00 USDT</strong></li>
</ul>
<p>The documentation also outlines vesting terms for pre-sale tokens, as well as other mechanisms aligned to provide sustainable growth stability for the project, rewarding long-term holders and early adopters.</p>
<p><strong>Broker Network and Market Positioning</strong></p>
<p>The global yacht charter and yachting services market represents a <strong>multi-billion-dollar industry</strong>, traditionally limited to a small group of high-capital participants. <strong>Investing Yachts aims to use its RWA structure to broaden access by enabling community participation through $YATE</strong>, bringing a token-based framework to a segment that has historically remained offline and illiquid.</p>
<p><strong>Investing Yachts</strong> has established <strong>relationships with experienced yacht brokers</strong> and industry intermediaries to support fleet sourcing and charter deployment. These connections are intended to strengthen the project’s ability to identify acquisition opportunities, negotiate terms, and access vessels aligned with demand in key charter regions.</p>
<p><strong>Community and updates</strong></p>
<p><strong>Investing Yachts</strong> is publishing updates via social channels and encourages supporters to follow the project for pre-sale announcements, documentation updates, and roadmap progress:</p>
<ul>
<li>X: <a href="https://x.com/Investingyachts" rel="nofollow noopener" target="_blank">https://x.com/Investingyachts</a></li>

<p><a href="https://investingyachts.com/" rel="nofollow noopener" target="_blank">Investing Yachts</a> is a blockchain platform described as an RWA project focused on tokenizing exposure to luxury yacht charter economics through the $YATE token (Ethereum ERC-20).</p>
<p>Investing Yachts lists a management team and advisory group spanning technology, yacht operations, finance, media, and international legal expertise. cryptopotato_1770742002000_3349741|1770742002000|2026|2|7|2026-02-10|cryptopotato|RAIN Explodes by 20% Daily, Bitcoin Stalls Below $70K: Market Watch|<p>Bitcoin&#8217;s price recovery attempts were once again halted at just over $70,000, and the asset now sits over a grand lower.</p>
<p>Most larger-cap altcoins have remained sluggish on a daily scale, aside from ZEC, which has jumped by 5.5%, and HYPE, which has dropped by over 5%.</p>
<h2>BTC Stopped at $70K</h2>
<p>The primary cryptocurrency&#8217;s recent price movements raised a lot of questions about the state of the market. The asset stood at $90,000 on January 28 but plunged hard in the following week or so. In fact, the culmination, at least for now, took place last Friday morning when it dropped to $60,000 for the first time in well over a year.</p>
<p>This meant that BTC had <a href="https://cryptopotato.com/bitcoin-erases-post-trump-election-gains-altcoins-crash-by-double-digits-your-weekly-crypto-recap/">lost</a> $30,000 in the span of under 200 hours. After such a calamity, it was expected that there would be some sort of rebound, which took place immediately on Friday. In a matter of less than one trading day, the cryptocurrency surged by $12,000 and tapped $72,000 by Saturday morning.</p>
<p>However, it couldn&#8217;t proceed further and <a href="https://cryptopotato.com/btc-price-wobbles-below-70k-wlfi-defies-monday-correction-market-watch/">slipped</a> below $70,000, where it spent most of the weekend. It tried to initiate another leg up on Monday but was stopped on a couple of occasions at $71,000 and $72,000. It has declined slightly since that local peak and now sits at $69,000.</p>
<p>Its market cap has declined to $1.380 trillion on CG, while its dominance over the alts stands firm at 57%.</p>
<figure class="wp-caption aligncenter" id="attachment_1428391" style="width: 1835px;"><a href="https://cryptopotato.com/wp-content/uploads/2026/02/BTCUSD-Feb-10.png"><img alt="BTCUSD Feb 10. Source: TradingView" class="wp-image-1428391 size-full" height="875" src="https://cryptopotato.com/wp-content/uploads/2026/02/BTCUSD-Feb-10.png" width="1835" /></a><figcaption class="wp-caption-text" id="caption-attachment-1428391">BTCUSD Feb 10. Source: TradingView</figcaption></figure>
<h2>RAIN Keeps Going</h2>
<p>Ethereum continues to fight to stay above $2,000 after a minor daily decline. TRX has slipped by a similar percentage as well. In contrast, XRP has jumped above $1.40 after a 3% increase. BNB, SOL, BCH, and ADA are also in the green, led by ZEC&#8217;s impressive 6% surge to $242.</p>
<p>HYPE, on the other hand, has dropped by 5.5% daily and now struggles below $30. RAIN has taken the main stage in terms of daily gains, having soared by almost 20% to well over $0.01. The other notable gainers now are NEXO, ASTER, and M.</p>
<p>The total crypto market cap has remained relatively still since yesterday at just over $2.420 trillion on CG.</p>
